# Connect Creator | Onlymonster Docs

Adding a creator is the first step to getting started with OnlyMonster’s management system. You only need to connect the creator once — after that, you can manage access for your team without ever sharing login details.

This guide covers creators without Face Verification. For Face Verification accounts, see the [Face Verification Login Guide](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/creator-adding-and-login-with-face-verification)
.

For a comprehensive overview of all supported platforms and available features, [click here](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/onlymonster-browser/supported-platforms-on-onlymonster)
.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/#step-by-step-manual-on-adding-a-creator)

Step-by-Step Manual on Adding a Creator


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Before you start, make sure you're using the **OnlyMonster Browser**, as it’s required for login and platform compatibility.

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/#adding-the-profile)

Adding the profile

1.  Navigate to the [Creators](https://onlymonster.ai/panel/creators)
     section and click the **Connect Creator** button.
    

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252Fm3nXsKt1aRk2IIXrwQEg%252FScreenshot%25202025-02-28%2520at%252015.24.33.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Decd0bc0c-5f41-4b1f-b8dc-d4df850eceb5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=49c05754&sv=2)

1.  Select the platform of the account you’d like to connect.
    

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FmQ5wFIkHoxu9wvZeYGuJ%252FScreenshot%25202025-07-16%2520at%252015.05.07.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6e502744-5f71-453c-b342-6dddc189ab28&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7376de5c&sv=2)

1.  Log in to the account you’re connecting by **email and password**.
    

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252F5o1FwaDXq64plODQkKai%252FScreenshot%25202025-05-22%2520at%252012.40.23.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D90ddec9d-b21e-420f-a58b-2fe82246f50f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=75bedbf9&sv=2)

Once the Login window opens, you have 15 minutes to log in the profile. If the timer runs out, refresh the page and start over.

If the page has 2-step authentication enabled via an authenticator app or SMS, enter the security code in the corresponding field.

If Face Verification is required, refer to the [Face Verification Login Guide](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/creator-adding-and-login-with-face-verification)
. The US proxies are already active on the login window.

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/#trial-period-activation)

Trial Period Activation

After connecting the account, you’ll be offered a 7-day trial with full access to platform features. Click Confirm to activate the trial.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FHuOtSvvSlNjyavkB1aWo%252FScreenshot%25202025-02-28%2520at%252015.34.39.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D04c067c9-8d2f-4381-a67d-ea53eceb539e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b7aaf0c7&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/#setting-up-creator-settings)

Setting Up Creator Settings

Once you activate the Free Trial, the Creator settings will open. You’ll be able to assign team members, set the proxy and time zone, and make other changes. By default, US proxies are enabled for the Creator. More details are provided in the [Proxy Management article](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/onlymonster-browser/proxy-management)
.

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/#process-complete)

Process Complete

The account has been successfully connected. You can verify this by checking the account status in the Creators section — an Active status indicates the account is ready for use.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252Fcm0lSs2EEZWNSD60TPbL%252FScreenshot%25202025-05-22%2520at%252013.01.04.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9bda76a2-68de-44ec-89d1-b91950d6b70e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d13d1d19&sv=2)

In case of a different status (Inactive or Waiting), please contact the Support Team via the chatbox in the bottom-right corner.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/#access-your-creators-page)

Access your Creator’s page


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The creator’s icon should now appear in the left sidebar. If the icon doesn’t appear, ensure that the trial is activated. (If you skipped the trial activation step - you can do it in the Creator Settings).

Click on the icon to access the profile.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/#deleting-a-creators-account)

Deleting a creator’s account


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To delete a creator’s account, please contact the Support Team and provide the creator’s ID (found next to the Creator's Icon), tag or link.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/#further-configuration)

Further configuration


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To customize the creator’s settings — please refer to the [Creators Management article](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/creator-management)
.

[NextCreator Adding and Login with Face Verification](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/creator-adding-and-login-with-face-verification)

# Creator Adding and Login with Face Verification | Onlymonster Docs

To add a creator account and complete login using Face Verification, follow the steps below. Make sure the creator is available and ready to complete the verification process in real time.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/creator-adding-and-login-with-face-verification#video-guide)

Video Guide


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/creator-adding-and-login-with-face-verification#steps-to-add-a-creator-with-face-verification)

Steps to Add a Creator with Face Verification


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  **Go to the Creators section** in your dashboard.
    
2.  Click **Connect Creator** and select the platform.
    
3.  Enter the **email and password** for the creator’s account.
    
4.  When the verification window appears, click **Verify with selfie** and select **Remember for 30 days**.
    
5.  A new window will open with a **verification link**.
    

*   **Copy the link and send it to the creator**.
    

1.  Ask the creator to complete the selfie verification **within 1 minute**.
    

*   Multiple failed attempts may result in a temporary time restriction.
    

1.  Once the creator has completed the verification, click **Complete** on your side.
    

Congratulations, you are done!

If you need help or run into any issues, feel free to contact our Support Team.

[PreviousConnect Creator](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/)
[NextCustom Proxy Setup for Account Connection](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/custom-proxy-setup-for-account-connection)

# Custom Proxy Setup for Account Connection | Onlymonster Docs

When adding a new account to your OnlyMonster agency, a proxy is automatically reserved. For certain platforms — such as **Reddit** — it’s crucial to use a custom proxy to avoid login issues, platform restrictions, or IP-related blocks.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FU90DVZthraXqy93RO9RF%252FScreenshot%25202025-08-18%2520at%252018.50.18.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D68427f81-9d38-4059-9882-e574c3c50ed5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2f5a8389&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/custom-proxy-setup-for-account-connection#how-to-add-an-account-using-a-custom-proxy)

How to add an account using a Custom proxy:

1.  Enable custom proxy: Toggle the "**Use Custom Proxy**" option before connecting the account.
    

_For Reddit platform, the credentials input window is always open._

1.  Enter Proxy Credentials: In the field, enter a **SOCKS5 proxy credentials**:
    
    1.  Host
        
    2.  Port
        
    3.  Login
        
    4.  Password
        
    
2.  Connect: **Click Connect t**o continue.
    

Once connected, the custom proxy will be **automatically applied to the Creator's settings**.

**Troubleshooting**: If you enter non-working proxy credentials, you'll receive a notification about the inability to validate the proxy credentials. Double-check that all fields (host, port, login, password) are entered correctly. If the data is correct and the error persists, it means the proxy itself is not working.

[PreviousCreator Adding and Login with Face Verification](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/creator-adding-and-login-with-face-verification)
[NextCreator Management](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/creator-management)

# Team management | Onlymonster Docs

**Adding employees**

For an employee to be added to the team, they first need to register on OnlyMonster platform.

You have to disable the built-in translator in your browser to complete the registration process.

During registration, they must select the **"I am an Agency Employee"** option and insert your **unique invite link****.** After that, they will receive a confirmation email.

To share the unique invite link, navigate to the ["Members"](https://onlymonster.ai/panel/members/)
 page, copy the link, and send it to the new employee.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FEHOWLLaTvArX3RTgKPVO%252FScreenshot%25202025-03-04%2520at%252020.02.50.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D39ca6b87-de41-4cfa-b441-615cd5ea915e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ded75741&sv=2)

Once your team members have successfully registered via your unique invite link, they will appear in your team members list.

[Role](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/roles-and-permissions)
 must be assigned to the employee before they can access the Creator page.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/team-management#managing-the-team)

Managing the team


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

With the ability to view the full list of your team members, as well as edit and delete accounts as necessary, you can efficiently manage your team's access and maintain control over your workspace.

**You** **can** **view all your employees at once, as well as use filters or a search field:**

1.  **Role filter** - each employee is assigned a role with chosen permissions (for more details please refer to the [Roles and Permissions article](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/roles-and-permissions)
    );
    
2.  **Tags filter** - you can add tags for additional team segmentation ([more details on adding tags](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/team-management#id-1.3-tag-or-delete-member-from-agency)
    );
    
3.  **Assigned creators filter**: Sort the members by assigned Creators;
    
4.  **Search field:** find members by their names or emails.
    

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FzIWCIWgbitaJrJaFPZKA%252FScreenshot%25202025-03-04%2520at%252020.05.39.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D244b71e0-ec1a-4899-9d93-cc614e6bf021&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=cb5ab4ba&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/team-management#general-view)

**General view**

**In the Team members list, you can view the following:** 5\. **Check box** - allows you to select multiple employees and assign them a role at once

6\. **Member’s ID**: A unique ID of each user

7\. **Member’s name**: Name that member specified when creating the account, or custom name if there is one

8\. **Assigned Сreators**: All creators assigned to the member. You can assign and revoke Creators by clicking on the icons.

9\. **Member’s email**.

10\. **Role** assigned to a member. **To each user's right, there are options to:** 11. **Edit** 12. **Remove the employee from the agency**

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/team-management#assign-creators-in-general-view)

Assign creators in General view

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FAjLhdpV1E3pHKw2CIcmv%252FScreenshot%25202025-03-04%2520at%252020.10.43.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4235d145-2b66-4ee2-907e-6489911a0555&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1b553e34&sv=2)

Clicking the icons in the **Assigned Creators** column will open the assigning menu. Here you can specify which OnlyFans profiles the employee will have access to, provide access to all profiles, or revoke access.

Choose a creator from the dropdown menu and click "Assign Creator" to grant access. To revoke access, simply click "Revoke." Use the "Assign All" or "Revoke All" options to manage Member’s access for all creators at once.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/team-management#edit-user)

Edit user


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

By clicking "Edit" you'll be forwarded to the member’s configuration page, where you can:

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/team-management#id-1.1-assign-members-role)

1.1 Assign Member's Role

Select a role from the dropdown menu, then click "Update" (for more details about roles, check the article).

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/team-management#id-1.2-assign-creators-in-edit-member-menu)

1.2 Assign Creators in Edit Member menu

You can specify which OnlyFans profiles the employee will have access to, provide access to all profiles, or revoke access. Select a creator from the dropdown menu and click "Assign Creator". To remove access, click "Revoke". You can simultaneously give or remove access to all creators by using "Assign All" or "Revoke All" options.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FDIG2ddU4bWLvZRbWHBuE%252FScreenshot%25202025-03-04%2520at%252020.16.59.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db95a5eee-cb9c-4b30-b631-6d1619dad5ef&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a71ac344&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/team-management#id-1.3-tag-add-custom-name-or-delete-member-from-agency)

1.3 Tag, Add Custom Name or Delete Member from Agency

The ability to tag employees allows you to assign tags to specific employees, which simplifies editing and managing them later. To add a tag, select it from the dropdown menu or (if you need to create a new one type it in the field, then click "Add as New Tag"). After that, click "Update". To remove a tag, click the cross icon and then "Update".

To add a **Custom name** - enter the name and click "Update".

[PreviousCreator Management](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/creator-management)

# Permissions Library | Onlymonster Docs

The permission system is a crucial element in managing your team effectively. Permissions assigned to a role determine which sections team members can access and what actions they can perform.

In this doc, you’ll find a brief description of permissions, categorized into four main areas.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/permissions-library#onlyfans-menu)

OnlyFans Menu


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This section includes permissions for standard OnlyFans functionalities.

*   **Home:** Allows team members to see the home feed, friends’ posts and stories.
    
*   **Notifications:** Allows team members to receive notifications from OnlyFans.
    
*   **Messages:** Provides access to view and engage in chats on the account.
    
*   **Collections:** Grants access to manage fan collections, including editing and clearing lists.
    
*   **Vault:** Allows access to the full gallery, including adding content to posts, stories, and categories.
    
*   **Queue:** Access to view and edit scheduled posts and messages.
    
*   **Statements:** Provides access to earnings, and chargebacks.
    
*   **Statistics:** Allows viewing of account stats such as engagement and performance.
    
*   **My Profile:** Access to view and edit the creator’s profile, including highlights.
    
*   **Settings:** Edit the profile, subscription pricing, safety settings, and notifications (safety-sensitive!).
    
*   **Streaming:** Permission to manage and run live streams (safety-sensitive!).
    
*   **Cards & Banks:** Allows viewing and editing of the creator’s banking information and wallet funds (safety-sensitive!).
    
*   **Help & Support:** Permission to contact OnlyFans support or explore Help Center resources (safety-sensitive!).
    
*   **Logout Button:** Allows members to log out of the OnlyFans account (safety-sensitive!).
    

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/permissions-library#onlyfans-chatting-and-security)

OnlyFans Chatting & Security


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Permissions related to chat and security functions.

*   **Chat Hiding & Fan Blocking:** Allows members to hide and clear chats or block fans (safety-sensitive!).
    
*   **Unsend Message:** Permission to unsend a message within 24 hours (safety-sensitive!).
    
*   **Add New Media:** Upload and send files from PC storage (safety-sensitive!).
    
*   **Download Media:** Permission to download media files from the Vault.
    
*   **Delete Media from Vault:** Permission to delete media and categories in the Vault (safety-sensitive!).
    
*   **Add stories:** Create and delete stories.
    
*   **Create New Post:** Create and delete posts.
    
*   **Create Mass Message:** Send OnlyFans mass messages.
    
*   **Promotions:** Permission to create and manage promotion campaigns (safety-sensitive!).
    

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/permissions-library#onlymonster-control-panel)

OnlyMonster Control Panel


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This block contains permissions for the OnlyMonster Browser interface.

*   **Dashboard:** Access to the central analytics board, providing an overview of key metrics across the organization.
    
*   **Chatter Metrics:**
    
    *   **View Metrics:** Access to Chatter Metrics dashboard - team performance statistics, including PPV sales, tips and message metrics.
        
    *   **View Transactions:** Access to Transactions tab without the ability to make changes. This permission automatically includes View Metrics permissions.
        
    *   **Edit Transactions:** Enables assigning transactions to agency members. Enables both View Metrics and View Transactions permissions.
        
    
*   **Chatter shifts:** Allows your team members to use a dedicated calendar to schedule employees’ work hours.
    
    *   **View shifts:** Only Viewing chatter shifts.
        
    *   **Edit shifts:** Create and edit chatter shifts.
        
    
*   **Creators:**
    
    *   **Connect Creator:** Permission to add creators.
        
    *   **Groups:** View and manage groups of creators, including adding/removing creators from groups.
        
    
*   **Creator Settings:**
    
    *   **Assign Creators:** Manage team members’ access to creator accounts.
        
    *   **Proxy Settings:** Manage settings for proxies, time zones, emoji customizations, and chat color splitting.
        
    
*   **Creator Insights:** In-depth analytics for creator performance.
    
*   **Traffic Metrics:** Analytical tools for tracking and trial links.
    
*   **Auto-Renew Promotion:** Access to the fan engagement tools for creating auto-renewing promotions.
    
*   **Auto-Follow Expired:** Manage auto-subscription settings for expired fans.
    
*   **AI Assistant Settings:** AI credits status, Status reply, and quick reply buttons customization.
    
*   **Media Hub:**
    
    *   **View Media:** Access to Media Hub files in the OnlyMonster Browser panel.
        
    *   **Upload Media:** Allows uploading media to the Media Hub panel using the “Upload Media” button (safety-sensitive!).
        
    *   **Edit Media:** Permission to create and rename folders, edit descriptions, tags, preferred prices, link and unlink folders.
        
    *   **Delete Media:** Allows the users to delete files and folders in the Media Hub panel.
        
    
*   **Restricted Words:**
    
    *   **View Restricted Words**: Permission to view Restricted Words tab in OnlyMonster Panel.
        
    *   **Edit Restricted Words:** Allows for adding and editing Restricted Words Settings.
        
    
*   **Members**:
    
    *   **View Members:** Permission to view members.
        
    *   **Edit Members:** Edit member information such as tags, notes, assign and revoke access to creators.
        
    *   **Remove Members:** Permission to remove members from the agency.
        
    
*   **Roles:**
    
    *   **View Roles:** Access to view and manage roles.
        
    *   **Edit Roles:** Manage role permissions and assign roles to team members.
        
    *   **Assign Roles:** Assign roles to team members.
        
    
*   **Agency:** View and edit agency information such as time zone and ID.
    
*   **Billing:** Access to billing, plan renewals, AI request usage, and billing history.
    

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/permissions-library#onlyfans-enhancements)

OnlyFans Enhancements


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Additional OnlyMonster tools for enhancing the chatting experience and fan interaction.

*   **Create Priority Mass Message:** Create and send OnlyMonster priority messages.
    
*   **AI Replies:** Access to create AI replies using quick reply buttons.
    
*   **Spell Checker:** Allows messages to be checked for spelling mistakes.
    
*   **Buying power:** Enables access to the Buying power (Fan Scoring) feature.
    

[PreviousRoles & Permissions](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/roles-and-permissions)
[NextFansly Permissions](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/fansly-permissions)

# Roles & Permissions | Onlymonster Docs

Some team members may only need to chat with fans, while others may require full access to manage the agency’s business operations.

In this doc, we will explain how to configure employee access using the roles’ system to ensure security and efficient operation.

Role must be assigned to the employee before they can access the Creator page.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/roles-and-permissions#h_fe6d24e8b2)

What is the Role’s System?


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Role’s system is a flexible access feature that allows you to control what your agency's employees can do. For each role, you can select specific permissions and save them. In this way, you create a pre-set of permissions that you can assign to your employees.

Thus, you don’t need to set up access for each new employee individually. Instead, you have to create the role and choose the permissions once.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/roles-and-permissions#how-do-you-create-edit-and-delete-roles)

How do you create, edit, and delete roles?


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Navigate to the 'Roles' tab. Here you can add a new role, edit it, or delete it if necessary.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FKbJpIcaZO4r0AVTfMEoS%252FScreenshot%25202025-03-04%2520at%252020.35.44.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D735a98b7-74ce-419d-81c3-9284aa87b171&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ec1e0a4c&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/roles-and-permissions#create-a-role)

Create a role

Click '**Add New Role**'

Name the role according to its intended function.

Choose a color for the role label.

Assign permissions to the role based on what access you want the users to have.

After you choose the permissions - click “**Create**”.

Done. The role is created.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FAhhzpzAcH6b130FJw0LF%252FScreenshot%25202025-03-04%2520at%252020.38.03.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da524a30a-d7d9-46d4-8803-f713b08a7bcb&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d8431747&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/roles-and-permissions#edit-and-delete-a-role)

Edit and delete a role

You can **edit** and **delete roles** in the Roles tab.

To change access settings for your employees, click "**Edit**". Now you’ve been forwarded to the **Permissions section**, where you can remove current permissions and grant new ones. After making the necessary changes, click "**Save**".

The role will be updated within 5 minutes, and all employees with that role will get the new access permissions.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252Fc0vniPc4enz8Io8jbHgO%252FScreenshot%25202025-03-04%2520at%252020.39.23.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D93c3dc9d-75e9-4949-8b1b-9a7b6d0a34ee&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e82c4ae8&sv=2)

To delete a role, click "**Delete**".

When a role assigned to a specific employee is deleted, the employee will be assigned the "**Default Member**" role. In this case, they will get access to the OnlyFans profiles and platform functionality. If you need to revoke all permissions for an employee, you can create a role with no permissions and assign it to employees as needed.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/roles-and-permissions#h_4660446df2)

General Permissions


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Permissions section contains all available permissions, which are divided into 4 blocks:

**OnlyFans Menu** - You can choose to either open or keep closed each section in the OnlyFans menu to ensure the security of your team’s operations.

**OnlyFans Chatting & Security** \- This block contains permissions related to the security of your agency.

Permission to Unsend messages allows a user to unsend a message within 24 hours. When disabled all users can unsend a message within 1 minute.

**OnlyMonster Control Panel -** Section access configurations for the OnlyMonster platform are crucial for managers and team leads, giving them access to analytics and management tools.

**OnlyFans Enhancements** \- Additional tools to enhance the chatting experience and fans’ interaction.

To grant permission, tick the corresponding checkbox. When all permissions are chosen - click on **Save**.

_These permissions are crucial for the account’s safety and they should not be given to all team members:_

_Settings_

_Streaming_

_Help & Support_

_Logout button_

_Chat hiding & Fan blocking_

_Unsend Message_

_Add (Upload) New Media_

_Delete Media from Vault_

_Promotions_

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/roles-and-permissions#recommended-by-onlymonster-roles-setup)

Recommended by OnlyMonster roles setup


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Recommendations for creating roles for both beginner and experienced chatters, as well as managers. These permission settings are recommended and can be used as a starting point for your work with OnlyMonster. You can select permissions based on your agency's policy and personal preferences.

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/roles-and-permissions#chatter-beginner)

Chatter (beginner)

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FarI8GOkBr2DNWUAVuUJH%252FScreenshot%25202025-03-05%2520at%252001.00.18.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D972d39b5-c872-4099-ae93-3e62fadf2b14&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=45e7917b&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/roles-and-permissions#shatter-pro)

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FPTr0QHNyLQzN1u9ijzLB%252FScreenshot%25202025-03-05%2520at%252001.01.03.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9d59d42c-1106-4d10-912d-51003e31fe89&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=562262d7&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/roles-and-permissions#administrator-or-team-lead)

Administrator or Team Lead

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252F0nlzBXbUUvheQJi7BFAa%252FScreenshot%25202025-03-05%2520at%252001.04.02.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd145718e-82ec-465a-a7f6-b915a41f7632&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a33f68f3&sv=2)

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/roles-and-permissions#assigning-roles-to-team-members)

Assigning Roles to Team Members


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Once you’ve created a role, you can assign it to employees in your agency.

Go to the [Members tab](https://onlymonster.ai/panel/members/)
.

Click on **edit member****.**

Select the role from the dropdown list.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252F7Q23DHeJWOjYgFJuKk9x%252FScreenshot%25202025-03-05%2520at%252001.12.06.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6718ecaf-7e7b-43b0-bac9-88a211812f8b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c8142f6e&sv=2)

# Creator Management | Onlymonster Docs

In the Creators page, you can view all creators and customize each creator’s settings. The OnlyMonster permission system allows you to control which team members have access to specific sections within this area.

In this article, we will explore the following areas: **Creators Management Overview** - Agency Creators List, allowing you to easily navigate to ➡️ **Creator’s Settings** \- Creator's customization tab.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/creator-management#creators-management-overview)

Creators Management Overview


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In the main section, you can see all creators added to the agency.

You can view all your creators or filter them by groups.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252F7SjyqMbXEXYm3JShQfld%252FScreenshot%25202025-02-28%2520at%252016.08.46.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dddfb821d-0d44-4625-8a0e-96a93e13b0f6&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=58ff38b5&sv=2)

Here you can also see:

1.  **Creator's** **ID**
    
2.  Display **name** and **username** on OnlyFans
    
3.  **Groups** they belong to
    
4.  **Subscription price** on OnlyFans
    
5.  **Session status**: **Active****;** **Waiting****;** **Inactive****.**
    
6.  The active **OnlyMonster plan**
    
7.  **Settings** - by accessing this section, you'll be able to fine-tune the creator’s settings.
    

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/creator-management#creators-settings)

Creator’s settings


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To edit a creator, click the blue **Open Settings** button in the Creators panel. This will take you to the **Edit Creator** section, where you can customize various settings.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252F4QIkqddUzABK9K8a62d8%252FScreenshot%25202025-02-28%2520at%252016.12.27.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D713a31d1-40b9-4b33-a3f2-e8d60166acb0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7a2edce3&sv=2)

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/creator-management#assigning-members)

Assigning Members


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In the **Members** section, you can see all team members who have access to the creator's profile. You can also **assign** or **revoke** access as needed.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FET2hFQnt9EteUMTzCARF%252FScreenshot%25202025-02-28%2520at%252016.14.48.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df8b35803-439e-4ae7-83dd-b58ba2f6633c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4d8c456e&sv=2)

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/creator-management#notes-and-groups-editor)

Notes and Groups Editor


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

On the left, you’ll see the creator’s **display** **name**, **username**, and **OnlyMonster ID**. You can make **notes** for each profile.

You can also assign the creator to a **group** for easy searching and efficient work in the analytical sections.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/creator-management#billing)

Billing


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

On the right, you’ll find the **creator’s plan** information and **expiry date**. You can select a plan by clicking the **Select Plan** button, which will take you to the [Billing](https://onlymonster.ai/panel/billing/)
 tab where you can manage plans and payments.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/creator-management#proxy-settings)

Proxy Settings


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This section lets you **manage proxies** for the creator’s profile - activate and switch proxy when necessary. We recommend activating the **Primary Proxy Provider**. For the best experience, choose a proxy from a location closest to your team. Active proxy is marked as selected. More information on proxies can be found [here](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/onlymonster-browser/proxy-management)
.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252F7VMRMFnAMyyVyayjtv1g%252FScreenshot%25202025-02-28%2520at%252016.18.42.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D05a292de-641a-4d68-8dd2-c2f334025c0d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fddd0d59&sv=2)

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/creator-management#timezone-management)

Timezone Management


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Managing time zones is crucial for coordinating your team. You can set an **Agency timezone** or choose a **custom timezone** for individual creator sessions if needed.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252Fm36iR5DTq5I3cHTqtKCc%252FScreenshot%25202025-02-28%2520at%252016.20.46.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D08426382-9592-4987-b012-596746d21fdb&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=20601469&sv=2)

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/creator-management#enhanced-color-chat-splitting)

Enhanced Color Chat Splitting


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If multiple chatters are working on the same creator's page, the **Color Chat Splitting** feature helps visually separate conversations by assigning distinct colors to each fan based on their **fan ID**.

You can enable **up to 6 different colors,** making it easier for your team to manage high-volume chats without confusion.

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/creator-management#how-to-use)

How to Use

1.  Go to the **Color Chat Splitting** section in the **Creator’s settings**.
    
2.  Select the **number of colors** (up to 6).
    
3.  **Switch the toggle** to activate the feature.
    

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/creator-management#to-customize-colors)

To customize colors:

*   Click any color block to open the palette.
    
*   Select your preferred color.
    
*   Click Update Color to apply changes.
    

Once activated, you’ll see a clear, **color-coded separation** in the **Messages** section.

For more details, see our [Enhanced Color Chat Splitting guide](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/enhanced-color-chats-splitting)

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/creator-management#emoji-customization)

Emoji Customization


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In this section, you can customize the **Emoji Bar**. The feature allows you to set a personalized emoji set (up to 15 emojis) for a creator. This ensures consistency across your team.

Click on the desired emoji so they will be added to the upper panel and click Update.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FZ9cTcELkgW4dBSmoy2Ks%252FScreenshot%25202025-02-28%2520at%252016.23.15.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbc2b253b-c797-426c-af55-0a6eeb7cae75&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ba652059&sv=2)

You’ll see the added emoji in the message section.

If the settings are not customized, team members will be able to add and remove emojis from the panel in the messages section on their own.

# Telegram Permissions | Onlymonster Docs

Below is a complete breakdown of permissions available within the Telegram integration. Each permission controls access to specific features and actions within connected Telegram accounts.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/telegram-permissions#account-settings)

Account Settings


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Settings:** Allows access to modify Telegram account settings such as name, profile picture, language, and notification preferences.
    
*   **Stories:** Grants the ability to view and post Stories from the Telegram account.
    
*   **Contacts:** Provides access to the account's contact list.
    

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/telegram-permissions#manage-chats)

Manage Chats


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Modify Chat Folders:** Enables creating and editing chat folders to organize conversations.
    
*   **Create Chats & Channels:** Allows starting new conversations and creating Telegram channels or group chats.
    
*   **Delete Chats:** Allows deleting individual conversations permanently.
    
*   **Archive Chats:** Enables archiving chats.
    
*   **Hide Archived Chats:** Allows hiding the archived chat folder from view.
    
*   **Hide Chat with Telegram:** Hides the system chat with Telegram (used for service messages and notifications).
    
*   **Hide Chat with Saved Messages:** Hides the "Saved Messages" personal chat.
    

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/telegram-permissions#contact-privacy)

Contact Privacy


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **View Usernames:** Allows viewing Telegram usernames of other users.
    
*   **View Phone:** Grants access to view users' phone numbers (if publicly available).
    
*   **Block Users:** Enables blocking contacts or users.
    
*   **Search Users:** Allows searching for users within Telegram.
    
*   **Create New Contacts:** Grants permission to add new users to the contact list.
    
*   **Edit Contacts:** Allows editing or deleting saved contacts.
    

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/telegram-permissions#in-chat-actions)

In-Chat Actions


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Delete Messages:** Grants permission to delete individual messages within chats.
    
*   **Forward Messages:** Allows forwarding messages to other chats or contacts.
    
*   **Schedule Messages:** Enables scheduling messages to be sent at a later time.
    
*   **Mute Notifications**: Allows muting or unmuting notifications for specific chats.
    
*   **Send Media:** Grants the ability to send photos, videos, documents, and other media files.
    
*   **Send Gifts:** Allows sending virtual gifts (if supported).
    
*   **Record Audio:** Enables recording and sending voice messages.
    
*   **Make Calls:** Grants permission to make voice and video calls via Telegram.
    

[PreviousFansly Permissions](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/fansly-permissions)
[NextManage Account Information](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/manage-account-information)

Last updated 3 months ago

# Fansly Permissions | Onlymonster Docs

Below is a full breakdown of permissions available within the Fansly integration. Each permission controls access to specific features and actions.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/fansly-permissions#fansly-menu)

Fansly Menu


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Feed & Leadboard:** Grants access to the content feed, posts and top creators list. When disabled, the member won’t be able to see updates or rankings like Top Supporters.

**Profile:** Allows for viewing and editing of the profile, including updating profile photo, bio, or links.

**Subscriptions:** Enables Subscriptions management (start, renew, cancel) and access to the Subscribers tab. When enabled, the user can subscribe to other creators or see their own subscribers.

**Lists:** Create and manage custom fan lists.

**Media Vault & Collection:** Grants access to the creator’s media archive, with the ability to upload content directly to custom folders and collections.

**Messages:** Grants full access to sending and receiving direct messages (DMs).

**Notifications:** Receive alerts for new messages, purchases, subscriptions and other account activity..

**Earnings & Cards**

*   **Earnings (Statistics):** View detailed breakdown of income (by time period, content type, etc.).
    
*   **Earnings (Wallet Balance):** View current wallet balance.
    
*   **Earnings (Payout Methods):** Set up and manage payout options. Enabling the permission gives access to updating or adding payout methods, as well as access to the Request Payout button.
    
*   E**arnings (Wallet History):** View full transaction history, including tips, purchases, and payouts.
    
*   **Payment Methods:** Manage stored payment options for subscriptions and purchases. Gives access to add, remove, or edit payment options for subscriptions or purchases.
    
*   **Referrals:** Access the referral system and performance tracking. Without this permission, members cannot view referral earnings or track partner traffic.
    

**Statistics**

*   **Profile Statistics:** View data on profile visibility and conversion rates. When disabled, member won’t be able to see insights about profile visits or subscription conversion data.
    
*   **Tracking Links:** Create and manage tracking links.
    
*   **Top Supporters**: Access to list of top-tippers and most engaged fans.
    

**Profile Settings**

*   **Plans/ Promos:** Set subscription prices and promotional discounts.
    
*   **Sessions Management:** View and manage all active login sessions and connected devices.
    
*   **Messages Settings:** Customize messaging behavior, including auto-replies, filters, restrictions and ability to unsent mass messages.
    
*   **Streaming:** Access live streaming features.
    
*   **Uploads:** Access to the Upload section in Creators Dashboard which allows for changing the watermark.
    
*   **Tax Documentation:** Access tax forms (W-9/W-8) and earnings reports.
    

**Settings:** Access general account settings.

**Guides & Support:** Access the help center resources and customer support. When disabled, Permission hides Contact Support, Help Center, Merch Store, Creator Guide, Terms, Privacy Policy tabs from the main menu, Chat icon from the top navigation bar.

**Logout:** Log out of the account.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/fansly-permissions#fansly-chatting-and-security)

Fansly Chatting & Security


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Purchase Media & Leave Tips:** Allows for purchasing content and sending tips to creators (safety-sensitive permission!).

**Change Online Status:** Toggle between online/offline visibility.

**Chat Hiding & Fan Blocking:** Hide specific chat conversations and block fans.

**Mute Fans:** Mute individual fans to stop receiving message notifications.

**Create Mass Messages:** Send messages to multiple fans simultaneously

**Delete Messages:** Remove specific messages or entire chat threads.

**Create New Post:** Publish a new post to the wall/feed.

**Create Stories:** Post and manage stories.

**Edit Profile details:** Change display name, personal details, and external links.

**Manage Walls:** Organize a content wall layout, visibility, categories.

**Edit & Delete Posts:** Modify or delete previously published posts.

[PreviousPermissions Library](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/permissions-library)
[NextTelegram Permissions](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/telegram-permissions)

# Manage Account Information | Onlymonster Docs

You can access these settings from any Menu tab by clicking on your **Profile Picture → Manage Account**

This menu is divided into two sections — Account and Security.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/manage-account-information#account)

Account


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In the Account section, you can update your account details and manage the emails linked to your account.

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/manage-account-information#customizing-account-details)

Customizing account details

To change your account details — such as your **profile photo, first name**, or **last name** — click on the **name bar**. You can upload a new profile picture from your device using the **Upload Image** button. Once you've made your changes, press **Continue** to save them.

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/manage-account-information#email-setup)

Email Setup

To add a new email, click **Add an Email Address**. After entering the new email, you’ll receive a confirmation code. Once confirmed, the new email can be used to restore your account if needed.

Clicking on the **email bar** will let you manage the email addresses associated with your account. You can designate one email address as the **primary email** or delete it from the account. If you delete your primary email, the next available email address will automatically become the new primary one.

The **primary email** will be used for logging in and receiving emails from OnlyMonster.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fstorage.crisp.chat%2Fusers%2Fhelpdesk%2Fwebsite%2Fe976c4b45fb54800%2Fimage2_1uk1xgc.jpg&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fc5320dc&sv=2)

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/manage-account-information#security)

Security


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In the **Security** section, you can change your password, enable two-step verification, and manage the sessions where your account is logged in.

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/manage-account-information#password-change)

Password change

To change your password, select **Change Password**. You’ll need to enter both your current password and the new one, then confirm it. You can **Sign out of all other devices** to log out of your account on all other devices once the password is changed.

If you forgot your password and need to reset it, check the [Forgot Password](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/forgot-password)
 article for detailed steps to help you out.

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/manage-account-information#managing-active-sessions)

Managing active sessions

In the **Security** section, you can view detailed information about all devices where your account is currently logged in. To log out from a specific device, select it and click **Sign Out of Device**.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fstorage.crisp.chat%2Fusers%2Fhelpdesk%2Fwebsite%2Fe976c4b45fb54800%2F1_s4qaxn.jpg&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4932d3bb&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/manage-account-information#two-step-verification)

Two-step verification

To enhance the security of your account, enable Two-Step Verification. To do this, click **Add Two-Step Verification**. Install a convenient two-factor authentication app on your mobile device and use it to scan the provided QR code. Once scanned, confirm the setup by entering the verification code from the app.

Be sure to download and keep a backup of the code. This will help you authenticate in the future if problems arise with the authenticator.

If you can’t scan the QR code, click **Can’t scan QR code?** and OnlyMonster will provide you with a **Key** and a **TOTP** link for your authentication app.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fstorage.crisp.chat%2Fusers%2Fhelpdesk%2Fwebsite%2Fe976c4b45fb54800%2F4_sitgce.jpg&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=76a34df2&sv=2)

**Two-step verification** adds an extra layer of security by requiring two steps to verify your identity: your password and a secondary factor, such as a code sent to your phone. This helps protect your account even if your password is compromised.

[PreviousTelegram Permissions](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/telegram-permissions)
[NextRestricted Words](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/restricted-words)

# OnlyMonster Browser Setup Guide | Onlymonster Docs

OnlyMonster Browser is a desktop application compatible with **macOS** and **Windows**. Installing this application is essential to gain full access to the platform’s features, including the OnlyMonster interface and OnlyFans accounts. This article provides a detailed setup guide for installing the OnlyMonster browser on Windows and MacOS.

System Requirements

To ensure the optimal performance, your system should meet the following specifications:

*   **8GB** of RAM or more
    
*   **Intel i5** processor (or equivalent)
    
*   **5GB** of free disk space
    
*   **50Mbps** internet connection
    
*   **macOS 11.0** (Big Sur) or later, or **64-bit** **Windows 10** or later.
    

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/onlymonster-browser/onlymonster-browser-setup-guide#windows-installation)

Windows Installation

Step 1: **Download the Browser**

*   Visit the OnlyMonster website’s [Download page](https://onlymonster.ai/downloads)
    .
    
*   Download the appropriate installer for Windows.
    

Step 2: **Locate the Download**

*   Navigate to your Downloads folder.
    
*   Find the downloaded `.exe` file.
    

Step 3: **Install the Browser**

*   Double-click the `.exe` file.
    
*   Follow the on-screen prompts to complete the installation.
    

Step 4: **Security Settings**

*   If a security alert appears, click "Run Anyway"
    

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fstorage.crisp.chat%2Fusers%2Fhelpdesk%2Fwebsite%2Fe976c4b45fb54800%2Fscreenshot-2024-09-13-at-16531_bxwyht.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c4659092&sv=2)

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fstorage.crisp.chat%2Fusers%2Fhelpdesk%2Fwebsite%2Fe976c4b45fb54800%2Fscreenshot-2024-09-13-at-16534_1oqucga.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=eba145e4&sv=2)

Step 5: **Check Firewall/Antivirus**

*   Ensure that no firewall or antivirus software is blocking the app.
    

Step 6: **Open the Browser**

*   Double-click the OnlyMonster browser icon on your desktop to open it.
    

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/onlymonster-browser/onlymonster-browser-setup-guide#macos-installation)

MacOS Installation

Step 1: **Determine Your Chip Type and Download the Correct Version**

*   Check whether your Mac uses an Intel or M1-M3 chip:
    
*   Click the Apple logo in the top left corner of your screen.
    
*   Select "About This Mac"
    
*   Under the Overview tab, look for the "Chip" or "Processor" entry to identify your chip type.
    
*   Visit the OnlyMonster website’s [Download page](https://onlymonster.ai/downloads)
     .
    
*   Download the macOS installer that matches your chip type (Intel or M1-M3).
    

Step 2: **Locate the Download**

*   Navigate to your Downloads folder.
    
*   Find the downloaded `.dmg` file.
    

Step 3: **Install the Browser**

*   Double-click the `.dmg` file to open it.
    
*   Drag and drop the OnlyMonster browser into your Applications folder.
    

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fstorage.crisp.chat%2Fusers%2Fhelpdesk%2Fwebsite%2Fe976c4b45fb54800%2Fmac_be9328.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=66f8dfc3&sv=2)

Step 4: **Security Settings**

*   If a security alert pops up saying the app can’t be opened:
    
*   Navigate to **Apple Menu > System Preferences > Security & Privacy** .
    
*   Under the **General** tab, click "Open Anyway" next to the message about the OnlyMonster browser.
    

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fstorage.crisp.chat%2Fusers%2Fhelpdesk%2Fwebsite%2Fe976c4b45fb54800%2Fmac2_qzsfzw.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3bf7f63d&sv=2)

Step 5: **Check Firewall/Antivirus**

*   Ensure that no firewall or antivirus software is blocking the app.
    

Step 6: **Open the Browser**

*   Double-click the OnlyMonster browser icon on your desktop to open it.
    

**Once installation is complete, open OnlyMonster and log into your account. The left sidebar will allow you to easily switch between the OnlyMonster interface and creator accounts.**

If the OnlyMonster Browser doesn’t run after installation, please refer to our [troubleshooting article](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/onlymonster-browser-troubleshooting-guide)
 for detailed instructions.

[PreviousRestricted Words](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/restricted-words)
[NextSupported Platforms on OnlyMonster](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/onlymonster-browser/supported-platforms-on-onlymonster)

# Restricted Words | Onlymonster Docs

Following platform rules is crucial for keeping your OnlyFans account active and avoiding potential blocks. A key part of this is using appropriate language in messages and posts. The platform can automatically block accounts for using certain words and phrases that violate its terms and conditions. To help prevent this, OnlyMonster offers the Restricted Words feature, that identifies and blocks banned words automatically.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/restricted-words#onlyfans-restricted-words)

OnlyFans Restricted Words


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

On OnlyFans, the Restricted Words feature does not always block messages automatically. If a word is on the platform's strict ban list, the message cannot be sent at all. However, for less restricted words, the message may still be delivered and appear in the chat before being manually reviewed by moderators. This can lead to several issues:

*   Chatters may unknowingly continue the conversation, being unaware that a message could later trigger sanctions.
    
*   If Platform moderators determine that the word violates platform rules, the account may get a warning or even be banned.
    
*   The account owner does not receive prior warnings, increasing the risk of unexpected penalties.
    
*   If OnlyFans protection is triggered, a message pops up, but it does not specify which word is a restricted one. This makes it difficult to identify the prohibited word. OnlyMonster, however, highlights the restricted word, making it easy to identify and address before continuing the conversation.
    
*   One significant drawback of OnlyFans’ built-in protection is the lack of logs for blocked message attempts. This makes it difficult to track and understand which messages triggered the restriction.
    

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FK0ag7x2EAHLoDLVYxKOi%252FRW%2520OF.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9c6c119d-35d4-4ce3-b77c-9cc683ff5b0a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3999e5f&sv=2)

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/restricted-words#how-onlymonster-enhances-restricted-words-protection)

How OnlyMonster Enhances Restricted Words Protection


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**The Restricted Words feature in OnlyMonster** is more reliable and customizable:

**Restricted words are fully blocked** — messages containing them cannot be sent by chatters. Agencies can **customize their restricted word list**, adding new words to align with their strategy. **A log of blocked message attempts is available**, allowing you to see which chatter tried to use a restricted word.

The Restricted Words feature is designed to:

*   **Automatically filter out banned words** and phrases to ensure compliance with platform rules.
    
*   **Enable custom word lists** for more precise filtering.
    
*   **Prevent account blocks** by alerting team members to potential violations before messages are sent.
    
*   **Track attempts** by team members to use banned words.
    

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/restricted-words#how-to-set-up-restricted-words-in-onlymonster)

How to Set Up Restricted Words in OnlyMonster


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Enable the feature:
    

Log in to your OnlyMonster account, open the Control Panel. Navigate to the [Restricted Words](https://onlymonster.ai/panel/restricted-words/)
 tab and activate the **Protection Status** option.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FBPAzpouLV5eKYY1JlmaP%252FScreenshot%25202025-03-05%2520at%252001.59.40.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da1e21a7c-5233-4039-adc2-1171857bf3c0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fc6615a0&sv=2)

1.  Use the preset list:
    

By default, the system includes a list of over 150 banned words that violate OnlyFans rules. This list will be automatically applied when protected status is enabled.

1.  Add custom restricted words:
    

You can add specific words or phrases to the banned list to suit your needs. When adding custom words, you can also block parts of a word by using the asterisk (\*) symbol. To block a word and its variations, add both the root word and derivatives.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FSFDmOL9fplFrDCXN4rZR%252FScreenshot%25202025-03-05%2520at%252002.00.38.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D375e5c00-73b7-4f15-be1b-e949ad6adf57&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ca370f48&sv=2)

1.  Additional protection:
    

This feature also includes AI-powered detection that can help identify unwanted addresses or links. It provides additional protection by allowing you to block websites, email addresses, phone numbers, and crypto wallet details.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252Fbzo7WWIIBVdibupvcb7H%252FScreenshot%25202025-03-05%2520at%252002.00.50.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2b11b429-c25e-4861-bc6f-988841e0644c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=48edb4cf&sv=2)

1.  Save your changes:
    

After customizing your list, click **Update** to apply the changes.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/restricted-words#how-to-check-attempts-for-restricted-words)

How to Check Attempts for Restricted Words


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Once the Restricted Words feature is activated, the system automatically checks all your messages, including private messages, OF mass messages, and OM priority messages. If any banned words are detected, they will be highlighted before the message is sent, allowing you to remove or replace them.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/restricted-words#restricted-words-logs)

Restricted Words Logs


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FS7saMCeWDpFhYjNTOjCI%252FScreenshot%25202025-03-05%2520at%252011.45.07.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dafe4b744-108e-47f1-a999-c8d5ce55e373&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=22a4053f&sv=2)

Managers with access to the Restricted Words tab can view the Restricted Words Log, which tracks the following details:

1.  The creator linked to the restricted word.
    
2.  The chatter who attempted to use the word.
    
3.  A link to the chat where the word was used.
    
4.  The type of message sent.
    
5.  The restricted word itself.
    
6.  The full message containing the banned word.
    
7.  The date the message was sent.
    

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/restricted-words#restricted-words-permissions)

Restricted Words Permissions


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**View Restricted Words**: Permission to view Restricted Words tab in OnlyMonster Panel.

**Edit Restricted Words:** Allows for adding and editing Restricted Words Settings.

[PreviousManage Account Information](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/team-and-security-management/manage-account-information)
[NextOnlyMonster Browser Setup Guide](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/onlymonster-browser/onlymonster-browser-setup-guide)

# Shift-Based Access Control | Onlymonster Docs

The **Chatter Shifts** feature now includes **access restriction** **controls** that let you define exactly when team members can access creator profiles. This helps improve security, reduce mistakes, and ensure chatters are only working during approved hours.

**When enabled, chatters will only be able to access profiles during their scheduled shifts.**

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/management-system/shift-based-access-control#need-help-setting-up-shifts)

Need help setting up shifts?

[Click here for step-by-step instructions on creating shifts.](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/management-system/chatter-shifts)

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/management-system/shift-based-access-control#whats-new)

What's New?


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Previously, shifts worked only as a scheduling calendar, but chatters could still access profiles outside their assigned hours.

With **access restrictions activated**, the system now enforces access rules:

*   Chatters **cannot open assigned creator profiles** outside their scheduled hours
    
*   Profile avatars will appear **grayed out with a lock icon** when access is restricted
    

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/management-system/shift-based-access-control#role-based-access)

Role-Based Access


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can enable shift-based access per role.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252F1yy2uCCF9Rz8h2YASFuE%252FScreenshot%25202025-06-30%2520at%252018.23.00.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1404b459-e8c0-4b97-8710-3621487264ff&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9e710305&sv=2)

Once enabled, all team members assigned to that role will only have access during their scheduled shifts.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/management-system/shift-based-access-control#countdown-timer-on-profile-avatars)

Countdown Timer on Profile Avatars


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

During an active shift, each profile avatar in the sidebar now displays a countdown timer indicating how much time remains in the current shift.

*   A green timer appears 5 minutes before the shift starts, counting down to the beginning
    
*   A red timer appears 5 minutes before the shift ends, counting down to the end
    

This visual aid helps chatters stay aware of their shift timing — so they can **wrap up conversations or request an extension** if needed.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/management-system/shift-based-access-control#how-to-enable-access-restrictions)

How to Enable Access Restrictions


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To activate shift-based access control:

1.  Make sure your team is using **OnlyMonster version 3.11.0 or later**
    
2.  Navigate to **Roles** in your admin settings, select the required role and click→ **Edit**
    
3.  Enable the toggle "**Allow access only during active shifts**"
    

Once enabled, chatters will only have access to creator profiles during their scheduled shift times.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/management-system/shift-based-access-control#shift-extension)

Shift Extension


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If a chatter is running out of time but needs to finish a conversation, they can extend their shift by 15 minutes directly from the Chatter Shifts panel.

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/management-system/shift-based-access-control#requirements-for-shift-extension)

Requirements for Shift Extension:

*   The chatter must have **View Shifts permission** to extend their shift by 15 minutes
    
*   The **Edit Shifts** permission provides access to creating and editing shifts for all creators the team member can access
    
*   The extension option becomes available shortly before the shift ends
    

This feature ensures better time management and prevents disruption to ongoing conversations while maintaining strict access controls.

[PreviousChatter shifts](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/management-system/chatter-shifts)
[NextChatter Metrics](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/management-system/chatter-metrics)

# Message Templates/Scripts | Onlymonster Docs

**Templates are essential for boosting productivity and efficiency for chatters, streamlining your messaging process and ensuring a consistent experience for your fans**

Create an **extensive library of templates**, each containing relevant text, media, and pricing options. This allows you to maintain a consistent tone and style in your communications and deliver the right content to your fans.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FouiqzphaYk0nfwVkmqx8%252Ftemplates%2520%281%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7fa47a17-842b-4afe-bc49-a2c9661bf331&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=946ade63&sv=2)

_Create a New Template_

Use **Template Tags** to quickly and easily locate the templates you need. These tags act as organizational tools, functioning like folders, to help you categorize and manage your template library efficiently.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252F8c3Wb7v6SbXoQjBl57Tt%252FT1%2520%282%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc220b190-dcec-4e3d-bedd-8394f9b5a345&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=39afa34b&sv=2)

_Template Tags&Folders_

Incorporate **notes within each template** to provide clear instructions or guidelines on how to use them. This helps reduce errors and misunderstandings, ensuring that chatters send the right content to fans.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252F43aaVQ7ywGxu1ITzw5xe%252FT2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4bfc2779-15a8-4f7b-802c-4e78afe61f4f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ea3b092f&sv=2)

_Template Notes_

Assign a **Sorting Number** to each template to control the order in which they appear in your chat with fans. This prioritization system helps you divide media sets into smaller messages/scripts, making them easier to find and use within your workflow.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FcGpsNfKwa14HTAPIBa0C%252FT3%2520%281%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfca9b3fa-82fe-4b9c-9bcd-0d7b5701e1ef&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4fd18601&sv=2)

_Template Sorting Number_

The Message Templates feature is an essential tool for streamlining your messaging strategy, offering **seamless synchronization** across all team members with a premium OnlyMonster plan.

This feature facilitates collaboration by allowing team members to share and access templates, fostering a cohesive messaging strategy across your fanbase. Provides flexibility for chatters to adapt and customize templates on the fly, ensuring personalized and relevant content for each fan.

# Message Tracker | Onlymonster Docs

Message Tracker is a feature in OnlyMonster that lets you monitor your team's chatting activity in real-time. It provides a centralized view of all messages sent by your team members, enabling you to oversee conversations and quickly navigate to any chat when needed.

This centralized monitoring system significantly improves management efficiency by allowing you to track messaging activity across your agency from a single location.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/management-system/message-tracker#how-it-works)

How It Works


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Messages appear in the Message Tracker within seconds of being sent. Even with a high message volume, all messages are loaded quickly and simultaneously, ensuring smooth real-time tracking.

Messages in the Message Tracker are stored **for 3 months** from the date they were sent. This allows managers to review past conversations and verify team interactions whenever necessary.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/management-system/message-tracker#message-tracker-overview)

Message Tracker Overview


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Message Tracker provides a detailed, real-time view of all messages sent by your team. It displays message data in a comprehensive table view, with built-in filters and precise information for each message.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FyjFkZ6VYm4V8snLz5HkA%252FScreenshot%25202025-10-16%2520at%252012.27.23.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D15d517d6-02d0-4fe3-9e2e-96782f8796ac&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=89f333c9&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/management-system/message-tracker#filtering-options)

Filtering Options

You can filter messages using the following parameters:

*   **Creator -** View messages sent from specific creator accounts
    
*   **Sender-** Filter messages by the team member who sent them
    
*   **Time Range** - The time range filter allows you to select the period for which you want to view messages
    
*   Price - Filter by message type based on paid status:
    
    *   **All** — all messages
        
    *   **Paid** — paid messages
        
    *   **Free** — free messages
        
    
*   **Reply Time** \- Filter by message response time
    

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/management-system/message-tracker#table-columns)

Table Columns

The Message Tracker displays the following information:

**Message -** The content of the sent message. If the message text is too long to display, hover over it to view the full text. Note: media previews are not currently supported.

**Sender -** The name of the team member who sent the message.

**Creator -** The creator account from which the message was sent.

**Fan -** The fan's ID displayed with a clickable link. Clicking the ID copies the fan's profile link to your clipboard. To open the chat with the fan, navigate to the OnlyFans profile and paste the copied link into a new tab.

**Send Date -** The date and time the message was sent, displayed in the user’s local time zone.

**Reply Time** - The time elapsed since the fan's previous message. If more than 1 hour has passed, this field remains empty, as this indicates the start of a new conversation.

**Input Method -** The method used to send the message. Available options include:

*   **Manual -** messages typed manually by chatters
    
*   **Copy-pasted** \- messages sent using copy and paste
    
*   **AI -** messages generated using AI Assistant
    
*   **Template -** messages sent from saved templates
    

**Price -** The price of the sent message (if applicable).

**Purchased -** Indicates whether the message was purchased by the fan.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/management-system/message-tracker#permissions)

Permissions


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Access to the Message Tracker is controlled through permissions.

Team members must have the Message Tracker permission enabled in their role settings to view and use this feature.

[PreviousTraffic Metrics V2.0](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/management-system/traffic-metrics-v2.0)
[NextMedia Hub](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/management-system/media-hub)
