# Creator Insights: Detailed Analytics for Managing Your Business | Onlymonster Docs

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FRKCuVnrjIGsVDseBBibi%252Ftg_image_612500856.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D669edef8-3485-450f-a614-f872e9ab35bc&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9ad6e8d&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/management-system/creator-insights-detailed-analytics-for-managing-your-business#customizable-filters)

**Customizable Filters**

*   Creator Selector – View analytics for all creators or select an individual profile for deeper insights. .
    
*   Time Range and Time Zone – Choose any reporting period and adjust to your agency's preferred timezone. By default, OF Time Zone (UTC 0) is selected. To use your agency's custom timezone, uncheck the box and adjust the setting in your Agency Settings. .
    
*   Earning Type Filter – Toggle between Net (after platform fees) and Gross earnings (before fees) for flexible reporting.
    
*   Synchronization Date – Displays the most recent date when the data was last synchronized and updated.
    

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/management-system/creator-insights-detailed-analytics-for-managing-your-business#core-metrics)

Core Metrics

*   Total Earnings – The total revenue generated in the selected time period.
    
*   Total Purchases – The total number of completed fan transactions.
    
*   Spenders – The number of unique fans who made at least one purchase. .
    
*   Average Earnings per Fan – Calculated by dividing Total Earnings by the number of Spenders — this shows the average amount each purchasing fan spent during the selected time frame. .
    

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/management-system/creator-insights-detailed-analytics-for-managing-your-business#visual-analytics)

**Visual Analytics**

**Earnings Chart** – Get a full breakdown of your earnings by category:

*   Subscriptions
    
*   Recurring Subscriptions
    
*   Tips
    
*   Posts
    
*   Messages
    
*   Streams
    

Use this chart to track revenue trends over time and identify which monetization streams perform best.

**Best Day** – Find out which day of the week brings in the highest average earnings within your selected period. You can filter by revenue type:

*   Subscriptions
    
*   Recurring Subscriptions
    
*   Tips
    
*   Posts
    
*   Messages
    
*   Streams
    

**Best Hour** – Discover the hour of the day when your fans are most active and most likely to spend.This metric shows average earnings per hour for the selected timeframe and is filterable by revenue type. Use this to optimize chatter schedules and campaign timing. .

**Day/Hour Earnings Heatmap** – A powerful visual tool to spot your most profitable time slots across the week.Each cell shows the average earnings for a specific day and hour. The lighter the cell, the higher the revenue.

You can filter by:

*   All revenue types
    
*   Subscriptions
    
*   Recurring subscriptions
    
*   Tips
    
*   Posts
    
*   Messages
    
*   Streams
    

Pro tip: Use the heatmap to time content drops, chats, and campaigns when fans are most likely to spend.

**New Fans** (single-creator view only) – Track acquisition trends over time.

Includes:

*   Paid and free regular subscriptions
    
*   Returning fans who previously unsubscribed and came back
    

Excludes trials, promos, and bundle-based signups — so you see real organic growth.

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/management-system/creator-insights-detailed-analytics-for-managing-your-business#earnings-breakdown-table)

Earnings Breakdown Table

Quickly see how your revenue is distributed across different income streams. Data is visualized in a pie chart to show each type’s percentage share of your total revenue.

*   Subscriptions
    
*   Tips
    
*   Posts
    
*   Messages
    
*   Streams
    
*   Other earnings
    
*   Recurring subscriptions
    

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FnhO1d4428AgKqxFZRvH4%252Ftg_image_3358694002.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D56027ddd-a525-4117-8994-a93e04cf119b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c2b672a1&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/management-system/creator-insights-detailed-analytics-for-managing-your-business#chargebacks)

**Chargebacks**

Displays:

*   Total number of chargebacks
    
*   Total value of chargebacks
    

Chargebacks are shown by the original transaction date, not the date the chargeback occurred — giving you accurate timeline context.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FnHmb73Bi76bjJGgQ4oer%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc08fec4e-e212-442f-8703-9a839f0727b0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3e1978e4&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/management-system/creator-insights-detailed-analytics-for-managing-your-business#additional-features)

Additional Features

**Top Spending Fans** – Get a clear view of your highest-value fans — sorted by total amount spent.

For each fan, you’ll see:

*   Number of purchases
    
*   Last purchase date
    
*   Average spend
    
*   Max spend
    
*   Total spend
    

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252Fg32kuaQAunshBG0ebtVY%252Ftg_image_3681813675.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D73fe5e19-46dc-4aaf-b292-e03b2ea598bb&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b40df324&sv=2)

**Export Option** – Download the top spending fans list in Excel or CSV format for internal analysis or reporting.

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/management-system/creator-insights-detailed-analytics-for-managing-your-business#conclusion)

Conclusion

**Creator Insights** is built on OnlyFans data and goes several layers deeper — giving you flexible charts, peak activity analytics, and a clear earnings breakdown. . This tool helps you evaluate performance from multiple angles and identify opportunities for growth.

The enhanced dashboard provides an intuitive way to track key metrics across your agency. To get the most out of it:

*   Track results **weekly or monthly**
    
*   Compare creators or campaigns
    
*   Use the data to tweak strategy, timing, and fan engagement.
    

This helps optimize processes, improve performance, and achieve better outcomes.

# Dashboard Overview: Comprehensive Metrics for Your Business | Onlymonster Docs

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/management-system/dashboard-overview-comprehensive-metrics-for-your-business#h_8c21589ad0)

Introduction


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The dashboard in **OnlyMonster** provides agencies, organizations, and solo creators with a comprehensive view of various metrics and indicators across their organization. The key feature is the ability to compare these metrics to understand process developments and identify areas for improvement.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/management-system/dashboard-overview-comprehensive-metrics-for-your-business#h_63b1bdedfb)

Main Dashboard Features


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/management-system/dashboard-overview-comprehensive-metrics-for-your-business#header-information)

**Header Information**

*   **Creators:** Displays the total number of active OF account profiles.
    
*   **Team Members:** Shows the number of active staff profiles.
    
*   **Spenders:** Indicates the number of fans who have made at least one purchase or tipped.
    

* * *

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/management-system/dashboard-overview-comprehensive-metrics-for-your-business#h_3017cefe95)

Filter Form


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/management-system/dashboard-overview-comprehensive-metrics-for-your-business#creator-filter)

**Creator Filter**

*   **Creator:** Allows you to select specific creators whose data you want to see on the dashboard.
    
*   **Multiselect Field:** Users can select multiple creators simultaneously. The default state is 'All creators'.
    
*   **Clear Button:** Clears all selected elements in the field.
    

_Group: This filter will also display groups of creators as separate entities for selection, allowing users to quickly choose a pool of creators that meet certain criteria. Grouping can be made by assigning specific tags to creators on the creator settings page._

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/management-system/dashboard-overview-comprehensive-metrics-for-your-business#time-range)

**Time Range**

*   **Main Time Range and Compare To Field:** Select the main time range and a comparison period to analyze performance across two different periods.
    
*   **Exact Time Selection:** Choose specific times in the AM and PM for precise data analysis.
    
*   **OnlyFans Time Zone:** Select the OF time zone to align your data with OF statistics. However, note that OF time range and data may sometimes differ from your dashboard data.
    

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/management-system/dashboard-overview-comprehensive-metrics-for-your-business#include-subscription-revenue-toggle)

**Include Subscription Revenue Toggle**

*   **Toggle 'Include Subscription Revenue':** Switch the toggle to include income from subscriptions. This is useful if you count subscription revenue in favor of your chatters.
    

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/management-system/dashboard-overview-comprehensive-metrics-for-your-business#informational-indicators)

**Informational Indicators**

*   **Data is color-coded:** green for growth and red for decline, compared to the range specified in the "Compare to" field.
    

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/management-system/dashboard-overview-comprehensive-metrics-for-your-business#general-metrics)

**General Metrics**


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

These metrics provide combined information from the selected creators:

*   **Total Revenue:** General income from all sources.
    
*   **Sales Revenue:** Income from messages and tips.
    
*   **Subscription Revenue:** Income from subscriptions.
    
*   **PPV Revenue:** Revenue from Pay Per View messages.
    
*   **Tips Revenue:** Income from tips.
    

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/management-system/dashboard-overview-comprehensive-metrics-for-your-business#specific-metrics)

**Specific Metrics**


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

These metrics offer detailed insights, including total and average information from the selected creators:

*   **Monthly Revenue Run Rate (RR):** Predictive metric estimating your total revenue for the current month based on daily earnings since the beginning of the current month.
    
*   **30-Days Revenue Run Rate:** Predictive metric projecting revenue for the next 30 days based on the last 7 days.
    
*   **Spenders:** Number of fans who made one or more purchases or tips during the selected period.
    
*   **APC (Average Payment Count):** Shows the average number of payments per paying fan.
    
*   **APV (Average Payment Value):** Measures the average amount spent per transaction.
    
*   **ARPPU (Average Revenue Per Paying User):** Tracks the average revenue generated from each paying fan.
    

* * *

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/management-system/dashboard-overview-comprehensive-metrics-for-your-business#h_f7ba7a6a17)

Detailed Metrics in the Dashboard


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  **Total Revenue:** Aggregated income from all sources over the selected period. This metric provides a comprehensive view of your overall earnings.
    
2.  **Revenue from New Fans:** Income generated from fans who subscribed within the selected timeframe. This helps evaluate the effectiveness of new fan acquisition strategies.
    
3.  **Revenue from Existing Fans:** Income from fans who subscribed before the specified period. Indicates ongoing engagement and loyalty from existing fans.
    
4.  **Like-for-Like (LFL):** Compares revenue from the selected period with the same period in the previous month. This helps spot seasonal trends and performance fluctuations.
    
5.  **Monthly Revenue Run Rate:** Predictive metric estimating your total revenue for the current month based on daily earnings since the beginning of the month.
    
6.  **30-Days Revenue Run Rate:** Predictive metric projecting revenue for the next 30 days based on the last 7 days' performance.
    
7.  **Subscription Revenue:** Earnings from subscriptions and renewals. Highlights the importance of recurring income streams.
    
8.  **New Fans:** Number of first-time subscribers during the selected period. Smart cloud automation works to attract and collect new fans.
    
9.  **Subscription Revenue from New Fans:** Revenue from subscriptions of fans who subscribed for the first time during the selected period.
    
10.  **Renewed Fans:** Number of fans who renewed their subscriptions during the selected period. Indicates the effectiveness of retention strategies.
    
11.  **Subscription Revenue from Renewed Fans:** Income generated from fans renewing their subscriptions during the selected period.
    
12.  **Sales Revenue:** Revenue from messages and tips, gauging the direct monetization from chatters.
    
13.  **PPV Revenue:** Income from Pay Per View messages. Provides insight into the effectiveness of exclusive content strategies.
    
14.  **Tips Revenue:** Income from tips transactions, reflecting fan satisfaction and support.
    
15.  **Posts Revenue:** Total revenue from posts during the selected time period. Percentage is calculated by comparing to Total Revenue.
    
16.  **Sales Ratio:** Comparison of sales revenue to subscription revenue, offering insights into the balance between direct sales and recurring income.
    
17.  **Tracking Links Income:** Performance of tracking links over the specified period. Helps optimize marketing efforts.
    
18.  **FTL Income:** Performance of trial links during the specified period, indicating the success of trial promotions.
    
19.  **FTL Fans:** Number of fans subscribed through trial links during the specified period. Indicates the effectiveness of free trial strategies.
    
20.  **Monthly Subs Run Rate:** Predictive metric estimating the number of new subscribers for the current month based on subscription trends.
    
21.  **30-Days Subs Run Rate:** Predictive metric estimating the number of new subscribers in the next 30 days based on the last 7 days' performance.
    
22.  **Spenders:** Number of fans who made one or more purchases or tips during the selected period, excluding subscriptions. Measures direct engagement.
    
23.  **APC (Average Payment Count):** Average number of payments per paying fan. Highlights engagement intensity.
    
24.  **APV (Average Payment Value):** Average amount spent per transaction. Provides insight into spending behavior.
    
25.  **ARPPU (Average Revenue Per Paying User):** Average revenue generated from each paying user. Crucial for understanding the value of your active fans.
    

* * *

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/management-system/dashboard-overview-comprehensive-metrics-for-your-business#h_ebb252aa42)

Additional Features


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/management-system/dashboard-overview-comprehensive-metrics-for-your-business#customize-columns)

**Customize Columns**

Click on **'Columns'** and select or unselect columns to display only the metrics they need on the dashboard, providing a corresponding view.

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/management-system/dashboard-overview-comprehensive-metrics-for-your-business#export-data)

**Export Data**

You can export all the data into a .csv file for further analysis or reporting.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252Fp1nJCC6b2JJgsiVk7fUe%252FScreenshot%25202025-03-20%2520at%252018.09.25.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1644d983-58ff-48ac-b7ac-8575404caa58&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9b4c15cc&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/management-system/dashboard-overview-comprehensive-metrics-for-your-business#sorting)

Sorting

*   Implement sorting by clicking on the column title or the arrow next to the title.
    
*   First click sorts data from highest to lowest.
    
*   Second click sorts data from lowest to highest.
    
*   Third click resets sorting to default.
    
*   Click another column title to reset the current sort and apply sorting to the corresponding column.
    

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/management-system/dashboard-overview-comprehensive-metrics-for-your-business#h_15bb358973)

Conclusion


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The enhanced dashboard offers a comprehensive and intuitive way to track, compare, and analyze key metrics across your organization. With the ability to analyze different time periods and groups of creators, as well as their traffic sources and sales, you gain valuable insights into your business performance. By understanding where your metrics fall short, you can identify the causes and consequences of these declines. Conversely, where you see improvement, you can recognize progress and the most effective management strategies, sales techniques, and traffic sources.

We recommend recording your results weekly or at least monthly, adjusting your strategy based on these insights, and continuously monitoring your progress. This proactive approach enables you to optimize processes, enhance performance, and ultimately drive better results for your organization.

For any questions or additional support, please reach out to our Support Team.

[PreviousMedia Hub](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/management-system/media-hub)
[NextCreator Insights: Detailed Analytics for Managing Your Business](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/management-system/creator-insights-detailed-analytics-for-managing-your-business)

# Enhanced Color Chats Splitting | Onlymonster Docs

When multiple team members manage chats for the same creator, distinguishing between different conversations can become difficult. The Enhanced Color Chats Splitting feature solves this by assigning distinct colors to conversations based on fan IDs, improving coordination and visual clarity across the team.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/enhanced-color-chats-splitting#whats-new)

What's New


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We've upgraded our color splitting system from a simple 2-color approach (odd/even) logic to a more advanced **multiple-color system** (up to 6) that provides enhanced visual clarity for larger teams.

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/enhanced-color-chats-splitting#enhanced-system-highlights)

Enhanced System Highlights

*   Supports **up to 6 distinct colors**
    
*   Uses a mathematical algorithm for even color distribution
    
*   Improves clarity and workflow efficiency for large teams
    

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/enhanced-color-chats-splitting#how-it-works)

How It Works


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The system calculates color assignment based on fan IDs using the following logic:

1.  **Take the fan ID** and divide it by the total number of enabled colors (up to 6)
    
2.  **If the result is a whole number** → assign the first color (index 0)
    
3.  **If the result has a decimal** → calculate the remainder to determine the color index
    

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/enhanced-color-chats-splitting#color-assignment-example)

Color Assignment Example

fan\_id ÷ 6 = result

If the result is a whole number:

→ Color index = 0 (first color)

If the result has a decimal:

→ Find the integer part of the result

→ Multiply by 6

→ Subtract it from the original fan\_id

→ This gives you the color index (1-5)

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/enhanced-color-chats-splitting#example-calculation)

Example Calculation

Fan ID: 300926977

1.  300926977 ÷ 6 = 50154496.1666...
    
2.  Since this has a decimal, we calculate the remainder:
    

Integer part: 50154496

50154496 × 6 = 300926976

300926977 - 300926976 = 1

1.  Color index 1 = the second color is used
    

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/enhanced-color-chats-splitting#setting-up-enhanced-color-chats-splitting)

Setting Up Enhanced Color Chats Splitting


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/enhanced-color-chats-splitting#enabling-the-feature)

Enabling the Feature

1.  Navigate to **Creator Tab → Creator Settings**
    
2.  Scroll to the **Color Chats Splitting** section
    
3.  Select how many colors you would like to use (up to 6 colors available)
    
4.  **Switch the toggle** to activate the feature
    
5.  The system will automatically apply the color algorithm
    

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/enhanced-color-chats-splitting#customizing-colors)

Customizing Colors

1.  Click on any color square to open the color palette
    
2.  Select your preferred color from the available options
    
3.  Click **Update Colors** to save changes
    
4.  Colors will be immediately applied to existing and new conversations
    

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/enhanced-color-chats-splitting#benefits-for-team-coordination)

Benefits for Team Coordination


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Improved visibility:** Six distinct colors provide better visual distinction than the previous 2-color system
    
*   **Faster identification:** Team members can instantly recognize which chats they’re responsible for
    
*   **Supports large teams:** Designed for high-volume creator workflows
    
*   **Even distribution:** The mathematical algorithm ensures relatively balanced color assignment
    
*   **Integrated UI:** Color indicators appear directly in the chat/message view
    

[PreviousVault Management 2.0](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/vault-management-2.0)
[NextFollow-Up Message](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/follow-up-message)

# Custom Emoji Bar | Onlymonster Docs

Using emojis can enhance your conversations and improve connections with your audience, potentially increasing fan satisfaction, loyalty, and revenue.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/custom-emoji-bar#h_5d036ac88e)

Personalize the Emoji Bar


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can easily customize your Emoji Bar via the **Edit** (1) and **Add Emoji** (2) buttons. This allows you to:

*   **Add your most frequently used and favorite emojis** for quick access.
    
*   **Streamline your messaging process** by organizing emojis that suit your communication style.
    

Customizing the emoji bar ensures that your preferred emojis are always at your fingertips, saving you time and helping you maintain a consistent tone in your messages.

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/custom-emoji-bar#h_5bd2bcb542)

Customize emoji for Creators

If you manage a team of chatters, you can **create a unified emoji bar for each creator**. This will keep fan interaction consistent among different chatters and emphasize your model's appearance and personality.

You can create an emoji bar the following way:

1.  Go to the **Creators** section.
    
2.  Select **Creator Settings** by clicking the **Open Settings** button.
    
3.  Scroll down to the **Emoji Customization** block.
    
4.  Select up to **15 emojis** that you want your chatters to use.
    
5.  Click **Update** to apply the changes.
    

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FYqdMBR9FMgmcVVQwsJHF%252FScreenshot%25202025-03-21%2520at%252019.31.38.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3869800d-0c85-438e-b664-1576527c5ff0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3eb4bee3&sv=2)

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FClH1YDjkJR5kcxu6roE6%252FScreenshot%25202025-03-21%2520at%252019.36.17.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da40d48e3-ef76-4f9e-88fc-2582ee3f85e2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8b0c8773&sv=2)

Once applied, all team members will use the same set of emojis for that creator, ensuring brand consistency across conversations.

When you customize an emoji bar for a creator, your chatters will no longer be able to modify their own emoji bar. However, they will still have access to the full list of available emojis from the general emoji set.

[NextEnabling Notifications on OnlyMonster](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/enabling-notifications-on-onlymonster)

# Vault Management 2.0 | Onlymonster Docs

For smoother and more advanced operation, we recommend using [Media Hub](https://onlymonster.ai/panel/media-hub/#)
 - a modern cloud-based media solution developed by OnlyMonster. Learn more about its features and advantages in our [article](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/management-system/media-hub)
.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/vault-management-2.0#vault-labeling)

Vault Labeling


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The media labeling feature allows one to easily track the status of content sent to fans:

*   Free: Content sent to the fan for free, marked in blue.
    
*   $value Paid: Content sent as a paid message and purchased by the fan, marked in green.
    
*   Unpaid: Content sent as a paid message but not purchased by the fan, marked in red.
    
*   Posted: Content previously posted on the feed, marked with “Posted” label.
    

The label system makes it easier to track content sent to fans, ensuring no duplicates and preventing double-posting.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FgLYPOmNsLRmlJO9uHZBQ%252Fimage%2520%2839%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc0eeaffd-2e9c-4ea3-a89d-9787f7ddf9bd&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=42ab76cf&sv=2)

_OnlyFans Media Labeling_

All media sent in the chat, along with their status label, can be checked in the Detailed Fan Info → Gallery Section.

Uploading the same media file twice results in duplicate copies. Only the version sent to a fan will be marked accordingly. To maintain clarity, use a single file per media and delete duplicates.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/vault-management-2.0#ppv-history)

PPV History


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

PPV History can be found in the Fan's Overview section. Here, you can view:

*   **A complete list of content sent to the fan**, including text, dates, and prices.
    
*   **Purchase statistics**, showing which content was bought or ignored.
    
*   Filters to display only **purchased content** or only **content sent for free**.
    

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FHM6cP2iMgFbc28DwjR7r%252Fvault2.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D175fa37a-0b9c-44ef-8d40-f42b46595e7c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=101f19c7&sv=2)

_OnlyFans PPV History_

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/vault-management-2.0#media-organization)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The option to edit descriptions and tags is available only for media files located in custom folders.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FNTrFEwy6ya8CrZkEujlJ%252Fvault3.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D76deff1f-cf13-4e9a-8cc6-09a7e75482fa&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=43efce23&sv=2)

**Tags:** Assign keywords to each media file for efficient searching.

**Descriptions:** Add a brief overview or context to each media file.

**Recommended Price:** Assign a suggested price to guide chatters during sales.

**View Attached Scripts:** the feature displays a list of scripts where the media is already included, providing clarity on its usage across various campaigns or messages.

_OnlyFans Tag Video Media_

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/vault-management-2.0#searching-and-sorting-media)

Searching and Sorting Media

With tags in place, searching and sorting media becomes faster and more efficient.

*   Use **specific tags** to **filter** your media library quickly.

# Advanced Fan Information | Onlymonster Docs

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/advanced-fan-information#fans-overview)

**Fan’s Overview**


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The **Fan’s Overview** widget allows you to view detailed information about the fan.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FzR5ou4TxZ3SnBwGjqQyj%252Ffans%2520overview%2520%281%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dad1f1467-6dd1-4e2f-9739-438eeac85895&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=54bfaf9c&sv=2)

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/advanced-fan-information#general)

General


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In the **General** block you can view the following information:

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/advanced-fan-information#name--username)

**Name + username**

Displays fan’s nickname and username in OF.

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/advanced-fan-information#country)

**Country**

Click to select the fan’s country. The system will display its current time to help your chatters communicate more effectively with fans.

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/advanced-fan-information#dob)

**DOB**

Click to enter the fan’s date of birth. The system will display the fan’s current age next to that field. Keep track of fans' birthdays to personalize your messages and strengthen the connection.

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/advanced-fan-information#fan-since)

**Fan since**

See how long the fan has been subscribed to your content.

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/advanced-fan-information#subscribed)

**Subscribed**

Displays whether the fan is currently subscribed.

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/advanced-fan-information#rebill)

**Rebill**

Displays the fan’s subscription rebilling status.

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/advanced-fan-information#last-online)

**Last Online**

Check the last time when the fan was online. If a fan hides their online status, it will be displayed as “Hidden”.

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/advanced-fan-information#last-response)

**Last Response**

Identify inactive fans by noting the day of their last response.

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/advanced-fan-information#last-read)

**Last Read**

View when fans last read your messages, filtering out unresponsive fans or using hook phrases to re-engage them.

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/advanced-fan-information#lists)

**Lists**

Displays the number of lists, to which the fan is related. Click to open the Collections → User Lists section in OF.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/advanced-fan-information#buying-power-section)

**Buying Power section**


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The **Buying Power** block allows you to view the fan's buying behavior. It consists of the following fields:

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/advanced-fan-information#buying-power)

**Buying Power**

This feature rates a fan's purchasing potential on a scale of 0 to 5. It helps operators assess the likelihood of future purchases and optimize interactions with fans.

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/advanced-fan-information#fans-spent-switch)

**Fans Spent Switch**

With this feature, you can view fan spending data either by individual creator or for your entire agency, providing a clear overview of their purchase history. The toggle enables you to effortlessly switch between Creator and Agency data, allowing you to monitor the following:

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/advanced-fan-information#spent)

**Spent**

View the total amount a fan has spent on your content, helping you understand their spending habits;

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/advanced-fan-information#avg-ppv)

**Avg PPV**

Displays the fan’s average PPV amount spent;

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/advanced-fan-information#avg-tip)

**Avg Tip**

Displays the fan’s average tip amount;

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/advanced-fan-information#purchased)

**Purchased**

Observe the fan's most recent content purchase, helping you tailor your sales strategy.

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/advanced-fan-information#chargeback-alert)

**Chargeback Alert**

This feature alerts you when a fan requests a chargeback, displaying the percentage of funds they’ve returned relative to their total spending. Powered by Big Data, the alert provides real-time insights to minimize risks and optimize your operations.

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/advanced-fan-information#view-ppv-timeline)

**View PPV Timeline**

Click to open a pop-up window with the total PPV history of the fan.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/advanced-fan-information#traffic-section)

**Traffic section**


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/advanced-fan-information#traffic-source)

**Traffic Source**

Select the web source where the fan came from.

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/advanced-fan-information#traffic-link)

**Traffic Link**

Automatically displays a tracking link if a fan has followed it.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/advanced-fan-information#preferences)

**Preferences**


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Select the fan’s preferences from the drop-down list.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/advanced-fan-information#widget-layout)

Widget Layout


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can **drag and drop** the **Fan’s Overview** window, positioning it wherever you find it most convenient on the screen. Additionally, you can easily **minimize or maximize the window** as needed, allowing you to manage your workspace while interacting with fans efficiently.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FCANe0Z7ZM0CJYjEQntu1%252FFO%25202.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1abe69b3-ad3b-4fb0-82f7-8ef9274a5776&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=94e33fed&sv=2)

Notes


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Team members can also **add specific notes about the fan**, which can be used for more personalized and effective communication, further enhancing fan engagement and sales.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FUbxJNQIsjV9o7OK5CdGj%252Fimage%2520%2830%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D28e38377-947e-4faf-9cdd-0fd75b90a199&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=19827dc7&sv=2)

Our team is continuously working on enhancing data collection and fan filtering capabilities, allowing chatters to make more informed decisions and boost sales. These improvements will provide valuable insights for your marketing team, helping to optimize your promotional strategies and effectively target fans. Stay tuned for future updates as we strive to bring you even more powerful tools to elevate your fan engagement and revenue growth.

# OnlyMonster Customization with CheckBox | Onlymonster Docs

By using the CheckBox, members can modify and add various elements for an optimized workflow.

This guide outlines the CheckBox settings and functionality to help you effectively customize your workspace.

The CheckBox is located in the **OnlyMonster Widget** on the Creator page:

1\. Navigate to the **bottom-right corner**.

2\. Open the **Settings** section.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FTCdhe6dS8Pu2N5bzofGh%252Ftg_image_1625069264.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd6e4d77d-b9cb-4902-9273-aa903059ea9b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2ec86116&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/onlymonster-customization-with-checkbox#general-settings)

General Settings

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/onlymonster-customization-with-checkbox#always-opened)

Always Opened

Keeps the Widget open after every page reload, opening a new tab, or launching the application.

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/onlymonster-customization-with-checkbox#hide-templates-in-messages)

Hide Templates in Messages

Hides the Message Templates window above the chat window when checked.

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/onlymonster-customization-with-checkbox#real-time-alerts-for-online-fans)

Real-Time Alerts for Online Fans

Enables in-app notifications for fans appearing online.

For more details, see the [Real-Time Alerts article](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/real-time-alerts)
.

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/onlymonster-customization-with-checkbox#mute-sound-for-online-fans-alerts)

Mute Sound for Online Fans Alerts

Mutes the sound for Real-Time Alerts when checked.

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/onlymonster-customization-with-checkbox#move-interface-layout-to-the-left)

Move Interface Layout to the Left

Shifts the interface to the left side of the screen for easier navigation.

When unchecked, the main interface is centered on the page.

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/onlymonster-customization-with-checkbox#minimalist-menu-view)

Minimalist Menu View

Removes text labels from the left sidebar, leaving only icons for a cleaner workspace.

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/onlymonster-customization-with-checkbox#translator-show-original-text)

Translator: Show Original Text

Displays the original text alongside the translated text when enabled.

Helps to provide better context by using both versions.

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/onlymonster-customization-with-checkbox#content-blur)

Content Blur

Blurs all media on the page, including fan icons, to ensure privacy while working in public places.

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/onlymonster-customization-with-checkbox#messages-settings)

Messages Settings

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/onlymonster-customization-with-checkbox#spent-badge)

“Spent” Badge

Adds a badge under the fan’s avatar showing the amount spent.

Helps prioritize chats with no need to switch views.

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/onlymonster-customization-with-checkbox#profile-picture-label)

Profile Picture Label

Replaces fan avatars with icons representing their status and behavior.

Reduces device load and enhances chat prioritization.

For details, refer to the [Fan Labels & Tags article](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/fan-labels-and-tags)
.

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/onlymonster-customization-with-checkbox#hide-muted-chats)

Hide Muted Chats

Removes muted chats from the list, keeping the chat window focused on active conversations.

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/onlymonster-customization-with-checkbox#hide-verified-non-spenders)

Hide Verified Non-Spenders

Hides chats with verified non-spend users from the list, such as creators with the same purpose.

By enabling and customizing these CheckBox options, you can create a streamlined, efficient workspace that aligns with your preferences and workflow.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/onlymonster-customization-with-checkbox#zoom-controls)

Zoom Controls


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Use **Ctrl + Plus/Minus** (`Windows`) or **Cmd + Plus/Minus** (`Mac`) to zoom in or out. This feature allows you to customize the display according to your comfort.

# Quick Reply | Onlymonster Docs

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/quick-reply#how-quick-reply-works)

How Quick Reply Works


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Go to the “**Notifications**” Section You'll see a Quick Reply option next to the notification.
    
2.  Click the **Quick Reply Button** A message window will appear, allowing you to type a quick greeting.
    
3.  Write Your Message and **Send** Once sent, the Quick Reply window will disappear from your notifications, and the fan will receive your message.
    

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252Fs6KjWqC0mnt2JXhJJBrb%252FScreenshot%25202025-04-08%2520at%252013.56.03.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcc738578-4cbf-4a81-b34b-8e9842d84cbe&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7765eade&sv=2)

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/quick-reply#after-sending-a-quick-reply)

After Sending a Quick Reply


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   One-time use: Once a Quick Reply is sent, the button disappears for everyone on the account, ensuring fans don’t receive multiple quick replies.
    
*   Continue the conversation anytime: A chat icon next to the Quick Reply button lets you open a full chat with the fan instantly.
    

By using Quick Reply, you can engage fans quickly and save time, keeping interactions smooth and efficient while leaving space for deeper conversations later.

[PreviousOnlyMonster Customization with CheckBox](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/onlymonster-customization-with-checkbox)
[NextAI Translator Overview](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/ai-magic-assistant/ai-translator-overview)

# Priority Mass Messages V2.0 | Onlymonster Docs

Priority Mass Messages is a cloud-based OnlyMonster feature that allows you to automatically send mass messages to fans' Priority inbox. A system of advanced filters allows you to fine-tune delivery and improve fan engagement.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/priority-mass-messages-v2.0#general-information-and-overview)

General Information and Overview


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

On the main Mass Messages page, you can select a Creator and view all Priority Mass Messages campaigns launched for that Creator.

To create a new Campaign, first select the Creator and click the New Campaign button.

Important: You cannot create a campaign without selecting at least one filter from the Fans Audience section. The online filter alone is not sufficient - campaigns with only this filter will not run.

Currently, Priority Mass Messages are delivered only to fans who have made at least one purchase on the Creator's account. This functionality will be expanded in future updates.

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/priority-mass-messages-v2.0#campaign-overview-section)

Campaign Overview Section

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FbHTIsvVYa4RMg8CXF9AP%252FScreenshot%25202025-10-23%2520at%252011.43.32.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D91cc876b-0417-47a9-b65f-cab63788c956&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d60d831b&sv=2)

The following information is displayed in the campaign overview:

Message - The content of the message

Status - Current state of the campaign:

*   **Sending -** the campaign is active and messages are being delivered to fans based on the selected filters
    
*   **In Queue -** the campaign is waiting in line and will begin once the current active campaign is completed.
    
*   **Stopped -** the campaign was manually paused and is no longer sending messages
    
*   **Unsending -** Messages are currently being removed via the Auto-Unsend feature, based on your configuration.
    
*   **Done -** the campaign has finished successfully, and all messages have been sent to the targeted audience
    
*   **Unsent -** the campaign was created, but messages were not sent (possibly due to configuration issues or manual cancellation)
    

**Progress -** Percentage of messages sent

**Audience Filter -** Displays selected filters for targeting, including sending conditions and exclusion lists.

**Sent -** Total number of messages successfully sent.

**Unsent -** Number of unsent messages.

**Price -** Price set for paid messages (if applicable)

**Purchases -** Number of purchases made from the campaign

**Earnings -** Total earnings generated from the campaign

**Attachments -** Number of media files attached to the message

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/priority-mass-messages-v2.0#understanding-campaign-progress-indicators)

Understanding Campaign Progress Indicators

These indicators help you interpret the status of your Priority Mass Message campaigns:

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/priority-mass-messages-v2.0#campaign-not-started)

Campaign Not Started:

*   Sent and Unsent columns display a dash (—)
    
*   Progress bar remains at 0%
    
*   Meaning: The campaign is configured but hasn't begun sending messages yet.
    

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/priority-mass-messages-v2.0#no-matching-fans)

No Matching Fans:

*   Sent and Unsent columns display a 0
    
*   Progress bar shows 100%
    
*   Meaning: The campaign ran but no fans matched the selected filters, so no messages were sent.
    

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/priority-mass-messages-v2.0#campaign-queue-system)

Campaign Queue System

Important: Only one campaign can be active at a time. If multiple campaigns are created, the first created campaign will start first. Other campaigns will be placed in a Queue and will only start after the active campaign is completed.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/priority-mass-messages-v2.0#setting-up-priority-mass-messages)

Setting Up Priority Mass Messages


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To create a Priority Mass Message, select Creator from the dropdown and click New Campaign.

You are now redirected to the Campaign Settings tab, where you need to configure the campaign settings.

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/priority-mass-messages-v2.0#delivery-options)

Delivery Options

To ensure smooth delivery, we process one campaign at a time. When multiple campaigns are scheduled for the same moment, they'll be placed in a queue.

You cannot create a campaign without selecting at least one filter from the Fans Audience section. The online filter alone is not sufficient - campaigns with only this filter will not run.

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/priority-mass-messages-v2.0#schedule-campaign-delivery)

**Schedule Campaign Delivery**

You can schedule your Priority Mass Message campaign to start at a specific date and time:

To schedule a campaign:

1.  Toggle "Schedule at" ON
    
2.  Select the desired date using the date picker
    
3.  Select the time for the campaign to start
    
4.  Choose the timezone reference:
    
5.  Agency - Uses the agency's configured timezone
    
6.  UTC - Uses UTC 0 timezone
    

Important: Scheduled campaigns will automatically start at the specified time. If another campaign is active when your scheduled campaign is due to start, your campaign will be queued and begin once the active campaign completes.

If scheduling is not enabled, the campaign will start immediately after you click "Start Campaign" (or be queued if another campaign is already running).

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/priority-mass-messages-v2.0#auto-unsend-message)

Auto Unsend Message

You can enable the Auto-Unsend feature:

*   Toggle "Auto unsend message" ON
    
*   Select the condition "If not read by fan" or "ALL"
    
*   Set the delay period (from 1 hour up to 20 hours)
    

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/priority-mass-messages-v2.0#fans-audience)

Fans Audience

Note: At least one filter from this section must be selected to create a campaign.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252Fy79Oro43l8ceFWs5Fp77%252FScreenshot%25202025-10-23%2520at%252011.46.58.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd5f9fbf9-91c2-477a-8e12-0cc064b8feb1&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=eaf508b3&sv=2)

When creating a Priority Mass Message campaign, you can apply the following filters to target your audience more precisely:

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/priority-mass-messages-v2.0#include-fans)

Include Fans

Fans matching these criteria will be targeted.

**Online Only**

Target only fans who are currently online.

**Subscribed from ... to ...**

Filter fans based on their first subscription date. You can set a date range for when fans subscribed.

**Spent on selected creator between... and ...**

Target fans based on how much they have spent on the selected Creator's page. When activating this filter, you need to specify both minimum and maximum spend amounts.

**Spent within current agency between... and ...**

Target fans based on their total spending across all models connected to the current agency. When choosing this filter, you need to specify both minimum and maximum spend amounts.

**Purchased from selected creator**

Filter fans based on recent purchases from the selected Creator:

*   Less than X days ago
    
*   More than X days ago
    

**Purchased within current agency**

Filter fans based on recent purchases from any agency model:

*   Less than X days ago
    
*   More than X days ago
    

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/priority-mass-messages-v2.0#exclude-fans)

Exclude Fans

Fans matching these criteria will NOT receive message.

**Active chats within the last**

Exclude fans with active chats within the selected timeframe (messages sent by the model only are taken into account):

*   Minimum value: 15 minutes
    
*   Maximum value: 24 hours
    

**Fan Lists**

Click here and select lists to exclude - you can select any number of exclusion lists.

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/priority-mass-messages-v2.0#create-message)

Create Message

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/priority-mass-messages-v2.0#text-and-emojis)

Text and emojis

Composing the Message: Enter your message text in the input field.

Click the plus (+) icon to open the emoji panel and insert emojis into your message.

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/priority-mass-messages-v2.0#personalisation)

Personalisation

To insert the fan's name or custom name:

Click the Dynamic Name button.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252Fhn55Lc6ShLbTY89Lf2XT%252FScreenshot%25202025-10-23%2520at%252011.48.05.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D930fa7c1-8ee2-4a1c-b93d-99011e0b1ede&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=45157ec0&sv=2)

Choose between the following options:

*   **Custom Name - Custom name** you've assigned (if available)
    
*   **Fan's Name - Name** from fan's profile (if available)
    
*   **Fan's Name → Custom Name** \- Uses the fan's name first. If it's missing, the custom name is used.
    
*   **Custom Name → Fan's Name** \- Uses the custom name first. If it's missing, the fan's name is used.
    

**First Word from Name**

When choosing Fan's Name - switch the toggle ON and the first word from the fan's name will be automatically inserted.

**Fallback Name**

Set a fallback name below to use when no custom or fan name is available. Use a warm placeholder like "Sweetie" or "Honey" when the fan's name isn't known.

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/priority-mass-messages-v2.0#adding-media-and-setting-price)

Adding Media and Setting Price

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252F0qnhANCfPAcqSpbtypIF%252FScreenshot%25202025-10-23%2520at%252011.49.55.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db87ea14d-f351-415f-ad69-1f633b3dfc06&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4cb8807e&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/priority-mass-messages-v2.0#free-media)

Free Media

To add free media to your campaign:

1.  Click the plus (+) icon in the Free Media field
    
2.  Select media from the media hub (media can only be added from the media hub)
    

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/priority-mass-messages-v2.0#paid-media)

Paid Media

To add paid media to your campaign:

1.  Toggle Paid Media ON
    
2.  Set the price in the Price field
    
3.  Click the plus (+) icon in the Paid Media field to upload
    

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/priority-mass-messages-v2.0#paid-text)

Paid Text

You can also create a paid text campaign:

1.  Toggle Paid Text ON
    
2.  Set the price in the corresponding field
    

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/priority-mass-messages-v2.0#before-launching-the-campaign)

Before launching the campaign

Carefully review all fields and settings. Ensure that at least one filter from the Fans Audience section is selected.

Important: Once the campaign is started, neither the message nor the settings can be edited.

When everything is verified, click Start Campaign to launch.

After launch, the campaign will appear in the campaign list with the appropriate status (Active if it's the first campaign, or Queued if another campaign is already running).

[PreviousAuto Messages](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/auto-messages)
[NextPriority Mass Messages](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/priority-mass-messages)

# Real-Time Alerts | Onlymonster Docs

By enabling these notifications, you can prioritize your time and focus on the fans who are active, ensuring that you make the most of your opportunities for communication and connection.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdownloads.intercomcdn.com%2Fi%2Fo%2Fksh6br93%2F1240370105%2Fe74e78e6f292295a7604162a0eb0%2Frealtimealerts1.png%3Fexpires%3D1732428000%26signature%3D7006cf83bcd58d313b4de50c5625df359d46c7a63f5ccabb97462572aff95f4d%26req%3DdSIjFsp5nYBfXPMW3nq%252BgUmEfAbl6tUKzwmDT1Dm7kgDQOd7P9JdTToVRJ7k%250Aiq63%252BZwFs8guMgkucU11h4HK194%253D%250A&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=67bde721&sv=2)

_Online Fan Alert_

Currently, we provide alerts for every fan coming online, but you can easily disable this feature.

Additionally, you can enable **notifications for specific fans** of your choosing for a more personalized experience.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FEGrt4P13ZPLuiu2MfMWJ%252Fimage%2520%2840%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6aeccaee-a6f6-433c-82fc-04fa13c165ab&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=77b4408f&sv=2)

_Real-Time Alerts Enabling/Muting_

**This feature is an essential tool for chatters, helping them stay on top of their interactions and maximize their efficiency during shifts.**

# AI Smart Enhancements: Customizing Onlyfans Chat for Natural Conversation | Onlymonster Docs

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/ai-magic-assistant/ai-smart-enhancements-customizing-onlyfans-chat-for-natural-conversation#lowercase-conversion)

Lowercase Conversion


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Effortless Casualness: Transform your entire message to lowercase with a single click. This mimics the casual, rapid style often seen in mobile messaging.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FUmLYNiWUrNMOazDwo4IK%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db5cbf318-814b-4d3f-9c48-14b04f419ddf&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a4cb33ce&sv=2)

Natural Converstion with AI Assistant

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/ai-magic-assistant/ai-smart-enhancements-customizing-onlyfans-chat-for-natural-conversation#comma-removal)

Comma Removal


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Fluid Conversations: Quickly remove commas from your message. This lends a more conversational, uninterrupted flow to your text, similar to natural speech patterns.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/ai-magic-assistant/ai-smart-enhancements-customizing-onlyfans-chat-for-natural-conversation#emoji-deletion)

Emoji Deletion


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Simplified Messaging: Sometimes, a plain text message is more appropriate. Remove all emojis from your message easily to suit the tone of the conversation.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/ai-magic-assistant/ai-smart-enhancements-customizing-onlyfans-chat-for-natural-conversation#shorthand-modification)

Shorthand Modification


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Authenticity in Brevity: Modify your messages with shorthands. This feature is great for creating quick, to-the-point replies that feel genuine and spontaneous.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/ai-magic-assistant/ai-smart-enhancements-customizing-onlyfans-chat-for-natural-conversation#writing-style-selection)

Writing Style Selection


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Personal Touch: Choose a writing style that best suits your or the creator's personality. This adds a layer of personalization to your interactions, making them more engaging and authentic.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FWzXNeYJi0JShwmY8l6JN%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da80e4ce0-cbb9-48ce-b1bd-9ea15ebea932&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d4652a4f&sv=2)

Ai Writing Styles

These smart enhancements are here to elevate your OnlyMonster AI experience, making your chats more natural, efficient, and tailored to your unique style.

# Enabling Notifications on OnlyMonster | Onlymonster Docs

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/enabling-notifications-on-onlymonster#how-to-enable-notifications-in-windowsos)

How to enable notifications in WindowsOS

1.  Open the **OnlyMonster** → right-click on the OnlyMonster logo → **Notifications**, and choose which notifications you want to receive:
    

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FqWYixTdD4VaQY5r644Md%252Fimage%2520%2814%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D26a22ab3-75ec-445f-9a06-5bbbda20bb59&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=58d2606&sv=2)

If needed, use the "**Disable All**" button to turn off message notifications for all profiles at once.

1.  Press the Windows key (⊞) or select it from the Taskbar, then go to **Settings**:
    

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXcbTKrFKcjRRQ-Jfnmg6VNWuDq6r81onidusYsEgXGNWST-vM7Iv48NIFuRGv0Ullg4F_FLIqzH2lXj9dDvtC72oZ9c0ER-YFX2xjbz7-lNez9t-oRzlL8T2uc9I8fbsfFwJsLJDXAvSvUONJPQ7t2WQeE%3Fkey%3DxwcFBaYwaM6CgQWJyB4HyQ&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=17f2ea24&sv=2)

1.  Navigate to **System** → **Notifications**, ensure that Notifications are turned on and "**Do not disturb**" mode is not activated.
    

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FRSfEnjZClMjz3YU6u0hz%252FScreenshot%25202025-03-21%2520at%252019.49.53.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8547dab7-05c8-4ccc-9b3c-ad6327051724&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f0ad85fd&sv=2)

Scroll down to “**Notifications from apps and other senders**”, find **OnlyMonster**, and turn on notifications for it:

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXc8VqulM1RiPF2ZAxmqj5c2zzRaz4f7hl025Hl91EaAgqG4qSfYzxLp-L6PtZ6QYdeWsy35GTcUjuI7kD5MtkLyO20g3LaEDd1CTCo3VWCCzUK6ol_UFmH6s_Y4iIfA5JTMA_x4zJDZB_fmF4Jd1raxX1aZ%3Fkey%3DxwcFBaYwaM6CgQWJyB4HyQ&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e28c1619&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/enabling-notifications-on-onlymonster#how-to-enable-notifications-in-macos)

How to enable notifications in MacOS

1.  Open OnlyMonsterBrowser → navigate to menu bar → Notifications → choose which notifications you want to receive.
    

1.  Ensure that **Focus** or **Sleep** mode is not activated.
    
    ![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXfoScefcuQXbplLGj3ftczN6714nZseirwz9TpI9RMdpy5bceNa3EIO2cXtszcLqxzRwLnz09V_KQN3G0vrhPB8k61m-61vce1igH0FsZpEqOL56Hj6EcX3oyRby0g5c3kTpM60cgbAkf3W2TCG_kue_Tk%3Fkey%3DxwcFBaYwaM6CgQWJyB4HyQ&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a54bcf6a&sv=2)
    
2.  Go to your **System Settings** → **Notification Center**.
    
3.  Make sure general notifications are enabled:
    
    ![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXdoeA8EU1rPy_STTSQVXTPcCAN5A3UaVZQ-AJYiNFamSmgV165WCMblqZ8LvxwvUdij_6F629k-EcM5WcvDif21NHcCJWVxsMPjavjCqDBDWPjvyVKew806krCFIXjDX8QIK2fRitlEWODcnjeJ0Om1okI%3Fkey%3DxwcFBaYwaM6CgQWJyB4HyQ&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=db174cee&sv=2)
    
4.  Scroll down and find **OnlyMonsterBrowser** → сlick on it, then toggle the switch to enable notifications:
    
    ![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXfFCy4pacJ4AS_OTTgDrNSIMbf4jcE1YufewuSyawr78I7Sm8mLAEi81sjYn89p91XOghhaz3aRl7eFwXX4We7q_5kLgxGAv6uvov7MtTG52HkWOO7ienNjhnb9miKBv_bkypw2gf1inwuO1rvyFuVw4LIb%3Fkey%3DxwcFBaYwaM6CgQWJyB4HyQ&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1a6ab100&sv=2)
    
    Choose your preferred notification style:
    
    *   Banners disappear automatically.
        
    *   Alerts, stay until you dismiss them.
        
    

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/enabling-notifications-on-onlymonster#what-information-notifications-show)

What information notifications show

When a notification appears, you’ll see additional information, such as the name of the model and a fan. Here’s what you can expect from different types of notifications:

*   **Subscriptions**: The name of the new subscriber
    
*   **Messages**: The text and the sender's name
    
*   **Purchases and Tips**: The amount and the name of the fan.
    
    ![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXeD-kH-GCDQllp9HFKua0NSMtsxLUcgfrcebAVNHQXhi1XSKLIGTqdOpJ2Ph8huLcsJXTZ0899tXcWc3j2hQli5S8xaFi7WOwl-R3v8Xmb0bFSuWWtt35bbi8x3EV5OHPSjcPIW4gpnNufp5dm4LqQ8jb8%3Fkey%3DxwcFBaYwaM6CgQWJyB4HyQ&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6153932f&sv=2)
    

You can close the notification by clicking the “**✕**”. For more options, click the **Options button (⋯)**, where you can either turn off all notifications or go directly to their settings:

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXccaxEuP1NBIu_OXo33Fz9G9sCt8iFPehX07qblNuFtvRpfhBzvO4nyGsqxmpQ1H0dmx0sAyBuKGH7GC8fByKl6wIWQYsqkL0pMvHp4uuSyQFl87n3DNW1R8oJ3aFSTLi0WYWEe_lsjc6Rvb-qLgSP6k0h5%3Fkey%3DxwcFBaYwaM6CgQWJyB4HyQ&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c4ff877&sv=2)

Please Note: The notifications will not appear if the fan’s tab is open. To receive notifications, you need to switch to a different tab.

# AI Auto-Generate Feature | Onlymonster Docs

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/ai-magic-assistant/ai-auto-generate-feature#step-1-access-ai-settings)

Step 1: Access AI Settings


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Open the AI Settings page for the specific creator where you want to enable auto-generated replies.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/ai-magic-assistant/ai-auto-generate-feature#step-2-enable-auto-generate)

Step 2: Enable Auto-Generate


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Choose up to two AI buttons for which you want replies to be auto-generated. Enable the Auto-generate feature for each selected button.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252F0uzpQAaklC3XE8bgwR5E%252F%25D0%25A1%25D0%25BD%25D0%25B8%25D0%25BC%25D0%25BE%25D0%25BA%2520%25D1%258D%25D0%25BA%25D1%2580%25D0%25B0%25D0%25BD%25D0%25B0%25202025-04-06%2520%25D0%25B2%252011.51.23.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db7cb7f32-d44b-4cee-9bc2-23cf21b498a1&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4cf94da2&sv=2)

OnlyFans AI Chat Bot

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/ai-magic-assistant/ai-auto-generate-feature#step-3-allow-syncing-time)

Step 3: Allow Syncing Time


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

After enabling Auto-generate, wait for approximately 10 minutes to allow the new settings to synchronize across the platform.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/ai-magic-assistant/ai-auto-generate-feature#step-4-enjoy-auto-generated-replies)

Step 4: Enjoy Auto-Generated Replies


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Once synced, the selected AI buttons will automatically generate replies each time you open a chat with fans, enhancing the efficiency of your interactions.

The Auto-Generate feature is designed to simplify your chat management, enabling you to focus on other important aspects of selling content.

Enjoy the blend of AI efficiency and personal touch in every conversation.

Keep in mind that while Auto-Generate simplifies the reply process, it's always good to review and personalize messages when necessary to maintain the authenticity of your interactions.

# Boosting Fan Engagement with AI-Powered Priority Mass Messages | Onlymonster Docs

Optimizing fan engagement is a key aspect of any OnlyFans creator's success. Our [priority mass messages feature](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/priority-mass-messages)
 is an innovative tool that helps you achieve this. Unlike the standard mass message methods that often get your messages lost in the spam list, our feature ensures your messages land directly in your fans' priority list. To take this one step further, we've integrated an AI assistant into this feature. It aims to help you create engaging templates for your messages, giving you a solid starting point for crafting that perfect message.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FmRvnR8uOV3Fb3IAxtpmP%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcafad37e-ccc8-4f58-a5c0-6dc7363b0383&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=12ca48f&sv=2)

Ai Powered Priority Mass Message

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/ai-magic-assistant/boosting-fan-engagement-with-ai-powered-priority-mass-messages#heres-how-it-works)

Here's how it works


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When you're composing your priority mass messages, our AI assistant will suggest a template. It's not a finished product, but more like a brainstorming partner giving you some ideas to get your creative juices flowing.

Remember, these AI buttons are a base for you to build upon. They're meant to be customized according to your specific audience and style. As with any message, it's crucial to test its effectiveness with your fans and fine-tune it based on their reactions.

Audiences are diverse and what works for one creator might not work for another. It's all about finding that golden ticket that resonates best with your unique fan base.

While crafting your messages, you can edit and customize the AI-generated text as much as you like. Additionally, to make your messages feel more personal, remember to use name placeholders. Personalization can go a long way in establishing a stronger connection with your fans.

Our goal with these integrated features is to make your messaging process as smooth and effective as possible. Use them wisely to maximize your engagement and your success on OnlyFans.

# “Too many requests. Try again later” Error | Onlymonster Docs

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FUOmghw4GFkVwgh779PaG%252FToo%2520many%2520requests%2520error.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D53f93da9-5498-4c05-aa6e-4456be85dc75&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=814532c2&sv=2)

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/too-many-requests.-try-again-later-error#understanding-the-issue)

Understanding the Issue


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Performing multiple actions on a Creator page, such as opening several tabs, frequently navigating between pages and other, can trigger the **"Too many requests. Try again later."** error.

If you exceed the platform’s rate limit, the error may appear repeatedly after every action.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/too-many-requests.-try-again-later-error#solutions)

Solutions


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Change Your IP Address** on the Creator Page
    

This error occurs when excessive requests are made from a single IP address. Changing your IP can resolve the issue.

To change IP, follow these steps: 1. Navigate to the **Creators** tab and open **Settings**.

2\. Locate the **Proxy Settings** section - **Primary Provider**.

3\. Click the Switch IP button next to the selected proxy.

For more information on **Proxy Management** - check out the [article](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/onlymonster-browser/proxy-management)
.

By following these steps, you can prevent the error from occurring and ensure a smooth browsing experience on the platform.

[Previous"Allow 3 seconds" Error](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/allow-3-seconds-error)
[Next“Session Synchronization Error”](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/session-synchronization-error)

Last updated 8 months ago
