# Priority Mass Messages | Onlymonster Docs

When you send a mass message on OnlyFans, it typically appears in the "All" tab, where fans may overlook it—especially if they follow multiple creators. Priority Mass Messages, however, stand out.

*   Fans receive a notification in the Priority tab.
    
*   If OnlyFans notifications are enabled, they will also get a push notification.
    

This makes Priority Mass Messages significantly more effective for engagement compared to standard mass messages.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/priority-mass-messages#message-sending-delay)

Message Sending Delay


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The sending delay sets the interval (in seconds) between each message being sent. Adjusting this delay helps:

*   Reduce device load
    
*   Avoid the "Allow 3 seconds" error (which occurs if OnlyFans limits are exceeded)
    

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/priority-mass-messages#recommended-delay-settings)

Recommended Delay Settings:

*   Up to 450 fans: 3 seconds
    
*   More than 450 fans: at least 10 seconds
    

You can adjust this setting based on the number of fans you are messaging to optimize performance.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252Fms8947uQyfbhzXB0ZCq7%252Fmm1.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De94b5994-6cd0-4f4c-b874-12a96ccf925a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=cb34c75e&sv=2)

Select Delay Setting

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/priority-mass-messages#personalization-with-name-placeholders)

Personalization with Name Placeholders

Make your messages feel more personal using name placeholders:

*   {name} – Inserts the fan’s chosen display name.
    
*   {displayName} – Uses a custom name you’ve assigned to a fan.
    
*   {displayName|name} - Inserts the fan’s chosen display name if a custom name isn't available.
    
*   {displayName|my friend} – If the fan has no custom name, "my friend" will be used instead.
    

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252F5sPOP45pvnMlti1TVN3n%252Fmm2.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5f9e5781-068f-4827-9a9b-f6224bfa6e05&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5c1ef1e2&sv=2)

Name Placeholders

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/priority-mass-messages#enhance-messages-with-emojis)

Enhance Messages with Emojis

Add personality to your messages with a wide range of emojis and search functionality. Click the emoji icon again to close the emoji window. To close the emoji window, click on the icon again.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FN8Bc0pOhIiJaafg5iZlM%252Fmm4.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D01fd6d93-f749-4e6c-b3b3-b11308ca9370&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=864519ce&sv=2)

Mass Message Emojis

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/priority-mass-messages#ai-assistant-for-mass-messaging)

AI Assistant for Mass Messaging

*   Choose from a variety of AI Assistant modes tailored to different messaging needs.
    
*   For a complete breakdown of AI features, check out our [AI Modes article](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/ai-magic-assistant/onlymonster-ai-2.0-a-guide-to-default-ai-modes)
    .
    

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252Fm1V9fUd73Syz8AKQQrcp%252Fmm3.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D88679f62-075a-4338-9b42-64bc268ba75a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=438d1b0c&sv=2)

AI Assistant

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/priority-mass-messages#adding-media-to-messages)

Adding Media to Messages

You can attach both free and paid media to mass messages:

*   Paid media converts the message into a PPV (Pay-Per-View) message.
    
*   Free media can be sent as-is or act as a preview for your PPV content.
    

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/priority-mass-messages#selecting-recipients-for-priority-mass-messages)

Selecting Recipients for Priority Mass Messages

*   Messages will be sent only to fans who are online at the moment of collection.
    
*   Fans with a hidden online status or expired subscriptions will not be included.
    

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252F7l8q5B061SgrCNvQydel%252Fmm5.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0645c5f0-d6fa-4b4e-a5da-097552f56018&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=abfe2112&sv=2)

Priority Messages to Online Fans

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/priority-mass-messages#select-and-exclude-recipient-lists)

Select and Exclude Recipient Lists

*   Choose specific recipient lists to include or exclude from your message.
    
*   If a fan appears in both the included and excluded lists, they will not receive the message.
    
*   If you’ve selected "Send to Online Fans Only," you can only exclude lists, not select new ones.
    

Use the [Lists Automation](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/lists-automation)
 feature for more advanced targeting!

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FnNqRFREH4gJjYyjyrtau%252Fmm6.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd10a3e4a-e4e8-49da-b2a2-21651ba79cad&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8a7eb3f1&sv=2)

Multiple Recipient Lists

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/priority-mass-messages#exclude-active-conversations)

Exclude Active Conversations

To avoid disrupting ongoing chats, set an exclusion period (1–12 hours) for fans you’re actively chatting with. .

*   An active chat is any conversation where the fan has recently sent a message.
    

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FGJswdyw6o99orc1XnvZF%252Fmm7.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3afc1265-1397-4514-b0d2-42db801ad2a6&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8e8c17fd&sv=2)

Exclude Active Conversations

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/priority-mass-messages#priority-mass-messages-history)

Priority Mass Messages History


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

All sent and deleted mass messages are stored in the Priority Mass Messages History section on your creator page. Messages only appear in this section after they are deleted.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FJ9rv3Itk5tmnFe0iyUPt%252Fmm8.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D06ccc7b7-0807-4fc5-83f0-9c46fa7e8970&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2b3f0263&sv=2)

Priority Mass Messages History

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/priority-mass-messages#technical-features-and-considerations)

Technical Features & Considerations


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Pause & Resume: You can stop sending messages at any time and resume later.
    
*   Unsend Within 24 Hours: Messages can be unsent within 24 hours of sending.
    
*   Local Storage: Mass messages are stored locally in your device’s cache.
    

You can close the tab, but the browser must remain open. Closing the browser may delete the cache, causing the message to disappear.

*   Device-Specific Visibility: Mass messages and settings are only visible on the device where they were created.
    
*   Lost Messages: If a mass message disappears from the creation menu, it was deleted from the cache and cannot be recovered or unsent.
    
*   Reducing Device Load: Increase the sending delay if message collection or sending is affecting performance.

# “Account Error” | Onlymonster Docs

An “Account Error” often occurs due to incorrect navigation to the site, browser issues, or problems with account verification or access.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fstorage.crisp.chat%2Fusers%2Fhelpdesk%2Fwebsite%2Fe976c4b45fb54800%2Ftelegram-cloud-photo-size-4-59_ah73xi.jpg&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b8cc71df&sv=2)

Account Error

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/account-error#solutions)

Solutions

1.  **Check the browser version**
    

Check your browser version in the top right corner. Download the latest version [from the website](https://onlymonster.ai/downloads)
.

1.  **Contact Support**
    

If the problem persists after trying the above steps, reach out to the support team for further assistance.

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/account-error#additional-tips)

Additional Tips

Make sure your browser is up-to-date to avoid compatibility issues.

[Next“Wrong Creator” Error When Attempting to Log Into a Profile](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/wrong-creator-error-when-attempting-to-log-into-a-profile)

# “Session Synchronization Error” | Onlymonster Docs

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/session-synchronization-error#understanding-the-issue)

Understanding the Issue

This error indicates a problem with maintaining a stable session, often due to browser or application issues.

Session synchronization errors typically occur when the browser or application fails to maintain a consistent user session. This could be due to a variety of reasons such as browser glitches, software conflicts, or session timeout issues.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FT87Xh8R1EN6CGP9gBqum%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2d14704c-ae4c-404b-9062-cc80159de9f3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=68304095&sv=2)

Session Synchronization Error

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/session-synchronization-error#solutions)

Solutions

1.  **Restart the Browser**
    

Completely close your browser and then reopen it. This can help reset the session and resolve synchronization issues.

1.  **Check your connection**
    

Ensure a stable and strong internet connection, as poor connectivity can contribute to such issues.

1.  **Contact Support**
    

If the problem continues after trying these steps, please, contact the support team for help.

[Previous“Too many requests. Try again later” Error](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/too-many-requests.-try-again-later-error)
[Next“Account Error”](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/account-error)

# AI Fan Persona - Insights from Chat | Onlymonster Docs

The AI Fan Persona Insights feature helps agency owners and creators gain a deeper understanding of their fans. By analyzing chat interactions, the AI identifies key personality traits, interests, and engagement patterns. These insights allow for more personalized interactions and content strategies, helping you build stronger connections with fans.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/ai-magic-assistant/ai-fan-persona-insights-from-chat#how-it-works)

**How It Works**


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The AI gathers data from chat conversations and generates a detailed **fan persona profile**. This profile includes:

*   **Common topics** of interest discussed in chats
    
*   **Emotional tone** and engagement style
    
*   **Personal preferences and behaviors**
    

By understanding a fan’s persona, you can tailor your interactions to better match their interests.

Once you review a fan’s persona, you can use the **Generate Reply** button to create a personalized response specifically for that fan. This AI-generated message will be closely aligned with the fan’s unique personality and preferences, making your communication more engaging and relevant.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FwsbBbTW2xjlvjIoQaJLV%252FScreenshot%25202025-03-06%2520at%252010.56.25.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db59da029-adf7-4e53-9bea-0967f86170eb&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3dc2a89e&sv=2)

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/ai-magic-assistant/ai-fan-persona-insights-from-chat#analyzing-fans-chat)

**Analyzing Fan’s Chat**


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

There must be at least 50 fan messages in the chat to create a Fan Persona. Ensure there are enough messages before proceeding with analysis.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FHAUhHkbykMjfXULSCflC%252FScreenshot%25202025-03-06%2520at%252010.58.57.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dea35bdda-e458-4a32-a9a4-49275ac8e678&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=238f66d4&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/ai-magic-assistant/ai-fan-persona-insights-from-chat#step-by-step-guide)

Step-by-step guide:

1.  Navigate to the **fan’s chat**.
    
2.  Select **Fan Persona** \- Generate Insight from the Fan’s overview menu.
    
3.  Use the information gathered by AI for your better understanding of the fan you are working with.
    
4.  Click **Persona Reply** to create a customized message based on the fan’s persona.
    

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/ai-magic-assistant/ai-fan-persona-insights-from-chat#ai-credit-usage)

AI credit usage


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Each Fan Persona generation requires 25 AI credits.

If you don’t have enough credits, you can [purchase additional AI credits](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/billing-and-pricing/payment-guide)
.

While AI Fan Persona provides valuable insights, it’s important to maintain authenticity in your interactions. Use this feature as a guide to enhance your natural communication style rather than replace it.

[PreviousAI Auto-Generate Feature](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/ai-magic-assistant/ai-auto-generate-feature)
[NextBoosting Fan Engagement with AI-Powered Priority Mass Messages](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/ai-magic-assistant/boosting-fan-engagement-with-ai-powered-priority-mass-messages)

# “Sync Error ‘timeout of 40000ms exceeded’” | Onlymonster Docs

**A synchronization error message stating “timeout of 40000ms exceeded” appears during browsing or attempting specific actions.**

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/sync-error-timeout-of-40000ms-exceeded#understanding-the-issue)

Understanding the Issue

A synchronization error with a timeout message usually occurs when the browser or app fails to receive a response from the server within the expected timeframe. This could be due to network congestion, server overload, or other temporary server issues.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fstorage.crisp.chat%2Fusers%2Fhelpdesk%2Fwebsite%2Fe976c4b45fb54800%2Fksnip20240527-153118_fucnra.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f313c7d1&sv=2)

Sync Error - Timeout

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/sync-error-timeout-of-40000ms-exceeded#solutions)

Solutions

1.  **Wait and Restart the Browser**
    

*   Wait for 5-10 Minutes: Sometimes, this error is due to temporary server-side issues.
    
*   Give it a few minutes before trying again.
    
*   Close your browser completely and then reopen it. This can help reset any stuck processes that might be contributing to the error.
    

1.  **Contact Support**
    

If waiting and restarting the browser does not resolve the issue, consider reaching out to the support team for further assistance.

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/sync-error-timeout-of-40000ms-exceeded#additional-tips)

Additional Tips

Ensure a stable and strong internet connection, as poor connectivity can contribute to such issues. Try accessing the site or performing the action during non-peak hours when server load might be lower.

[Previous“Wrong Creator” Error When Attempting to Log Into a Profile](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/wrong-creator-error-when-attempting-to-log-into-a-profile)
[Next“DiscardVirtualMemory” Error](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/discardvirtualmemory-error)

# Plans and Pricing | Onlymonster Docs

At OnlyMonster, we strive to provide not just an effective toolset for OnlyFans management, but also a transparent and fair pricing policy.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/billing-and-pricing/plans-and-pricing#pricing-based-on-creators-earnings)

**Pricing based on Creator's Earnings**


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Our pricing model is linked to the earnings of the creator you manage. As the earnings of a creator increase, so does the amount of data we handle, and the server resources we need to allocate. By tying our pricing to your creator's earnings, we ensure that you pay a fair price relative to the value you're getting from our service.

**Plan duration:** Each subscription lasts 30 days.

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/billing-and-pricing/plans-and-pricing#cost-of-services)

Cost of services

You can estimate the cost of services in advance using our [Interactive Calculator](https://onlymonster.ai/pricing#:~:text=calculate%20your%20costs)

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/billing-and-pricing/plans-and-pricing#payment-post-connection)

**Payment Post Connection**


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can pay for a creator after you've connected them and installed our OnlyMonster Browser. We then analyze the creator's earnings for the past 30 days to determine the pricing tier.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/billing-and-pricing/plans-and-pricing#switching-to-pro-plan)

**Switching to Pro Plan**


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you're on a trial and want to switch to a Pro Plan, you can easily do so by clicking on the button indicating your current plan, or by visiting the creator's settings and selecting the desired plan.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/billing-and-pricing/plans-and-pricing#no-recurring-payments)

**No Recurring Payments**


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Our pricing structure doesn't involve recurring payments. Instead, you pay in advance for 1, 3, or 6 months. This upfront payment system gives you the freedom to plan your expenses and manage your budget effectively.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/billing-and-pricing/plans-and-pricing#prepayment-benefits)

**Prepayment Benefits**


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you choose to pay for 3 or 6 months in advance, we won't charge you extra if your creator's earnings increase during that period. This way, you can lock in your current rate and protect yourself from potential price increases.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/billing-and-pricing/plans-and-pricing#flexible-payment-solutions)

**Flexible Payment Solutions**


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you encounter any issues or want to pay using a different method, don't hesitate to reach out to our support team. We're here to assist you and make your experience with OnlyMonster as smooth and efficient as possible. We currently accept payments through credit cards and cryptocurrencies for your convenience.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/billing-and-pricing/plans-and-pricing#book-a-demo)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

.

# AI Translator Overview | Onlymonster Docs

**Note:** Translation is available on OnlyFans, Fansly and Telegram.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/ai-magic-assistant/ai-translator-overview#full-chat-translation)

Full Chat Translation


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Full Chat Translation automatically translates all messages in a conversation, including both past messages and new incoming ones.

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/ai-magic-assistant/ai-translator-overview#how-to-use)

How to Use:

1.  Open any chat conversation.
    
2.  Click on the **Translation widget** on the right-hand side.
    
3.  Select the target language from the dropdown.
    
4.  Toggle **"Show Original Text"** ON to display both original and translated messages side by side, or leave it OFF to show translations only.
    
5.  Click **"Enable Translation"**.
    

Once enabled, the full conversation will translate immediately. All new messages will continue to appear in your selected language.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FDeYZVJBafukLGXWCrwd5%252Ftg_image_911884637.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D275cd71d-1d34-4637-87ab-6557756d8834&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9d25d62c&sv=2)

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FM3Uz5WXzOufQo4uPqwLP%252Ftg_image_3020135390.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6778ed6b-c7f5-4c4e-b0b3-5f6af74ebdd7&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=23e24bee&sv=2)

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/ai-magic-assistant/ai-translator-overview#translate-individual-messages)

Translate Individual Messages


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This feature lets you translate one message at a time, giving you full control over which content to translate. .

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/ai-magic-assistant/ai-translator-overview#how-to-use-1)

How to Use:

1.  Open any chat conversation.
    
2.  Click the **Translation widget** on the right.
    
3.  Select your target language from the dropdown.
    
4.  Click **"Translate"** beneath any message you want to translate.
    

This allows you to translate messages individually, giving you more control and enabling tailored communication for each chat message.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FU36trL281mttmyR0v5rw%252Ftg_image_220167286.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D23b925da-2702-4edc-ab17-cc3d34080808&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3e3e91ec&sv=2)

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/ai-magic-assistant/ai-translator-overview#outgoing-message-translation)

Outgoing Message Translation


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Outgoing Message Translation helps chatters instantly translate their messages into other languages before sending, ensuring clear and natural communication with fans worldwide.

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/ai-magic-assistant/ai-translator-overview#translation-modes)

Translation Modes

There are two modes available:

*   **Default Mode** — Provides direct, grammatical translation. This mode works for a wide range of language pairs and ensures clear, literal meaning. Default mode delivers accurate, word-for-word translations that maintain the original structure and tone of your message. It is ideal for straightforward communication where precision and clarity are the priority.
    
*   **Native Mode** — This mode transforms your text into natural, conversational speech that sounds authentic and engaging. Instead of literal word-for-word translation, Native Mode creates messages that feel human, lively, and culturally appropriate. This mode prioritizes naturalness and emotional tone over strict grammatical accuracy, making your messages feel authentic and emotionally resonant.
    

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/ai-magic-assistant/ai-translator-overview#how-to-use-2)

How to Use

1.  Open any chat conversation.
    
2.  Start by typing your message in the input field.
    
3.  Click on the **Translation widget**.
    
4.  Choose the **source language** (the language your message is written in) and the **target language** (the language you want it to be translated into).
    

**Important Note:** Selecting the correct source language is recommended. Auto-detection may occasionally misidentify semantically similar languages, which can affect translation accuracy.

1.  Select your preferred translation (Default or Native, if available for your language pair) style and click **"Paste"** to apply and save the settings.
    

Once configured, your translation settings are preserved. Every time you use the Translation widget, your message will be automatically translated according to your saved preferences. These settings persist even after restarting OnlyMonster.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FsbmDWJM5RG83fK2jW2BF%252Ftg_image_1778375438.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D15e21c10-40e9-44e8-960f-b5e70ccf2ac9&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=791480f4&sv=2)

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/ai-magic-assistant/ai-translator-overview#keyboard-shortcuts)

Keyboard Shortcuts


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/ai-magic-assistant/ai-translator-overview#windows)

Windows:

Alt + A - Translate with preview (keeps original text in input field for review)

Alt + S - Translate and auto-paste (immediately replaces input with translated text)

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/ai-magic-assistant/ai-translator-overview#macos)

MacOS:

Option + A - Translate with preview (keeps original text in input field for review) Option + S - Translate and auto-paste (immediately replaces input with translated text) When using the **preview shortcut** (Alt/Option + A), your original text remains visible in the input field, allowing you to review the translation before pasting it. The **auto-paste shortcut** (Alt/Option + S) instantly replaces your original text with the translated version for immediate sending.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/ai-magic-assistant/ai-translator-overview#mass-messages-and-posts-translation)

Mass Messages and Posts Translation


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The AI Translator is also available when composing OnlyFans Mass Messages and Posts, enabling you to reach a global audience effectively. Use it to:

*   Translate campaign messages
    
*   Localize posts for international fans
    
*   Reach a broader audience with culturally relevant language.
    

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FkQoG6hKmA0ha8ExuogBD%252Ftg_image_1370876242.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8309424e-54cf-436a-a722-8dbebf93e963&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=57064e7b&sv=2)

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/ai-magic-assistant/ai-translator-overview#supported-languages)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

####

**Default Mode**

All language pairs below are mutually translatable in both directions. These languages are available in Full Chat Translation, Individual Message Translation, and Default mode for Outgoing Message Translation.

*   Bulgarian
    
*   Czech
    
*   German
    
*   Greek
    
*   English
    
*   Finnish

# Advanced OnlyMonster Settings for troubleshooting | Onlymonster Docs

If you're experiencing performance issues or OF loading issues due to local restrictions, adjusting specific settings can help. Below, we explain three advanced options: **Disable OnlyFans Proxy Bypass**, **Disable OnlyFans JavaScript Cache**, and **Disable Hardware Acceleration**.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/advanced-onlymonster-settings-for-troubleshooting#disable-onlyfans-proxy-bypass)

Disable OnlyFans Proxy Bypass


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This setting determines whether some static OnlyFans files can be loaded directly through the IP of the user's device (without proxy). It helps speed up page loading, but may cause loading issues in regions where OnlyFans is blocked.

*   **Default State:** **Enabled**
    
*   **When to Disable**: If OnlyFans is blocked in your country, and you need all resources to load through a proxy.
    
*   **Effects**: Disabling this ensures all files load via the proxy. It does not impact vault loading and won’t cause any harm to the account.
    

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/advanced-onlymonster-settings-for-troubleshooting#disable-onlyfans-javascript-cache)

Disable OnlyFans JavaScript Cache


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

JavaScript caching allows OnlyFans to store and reuse JavaScript files, improving performance and loading speed.

*   **Default State:** **Disabled** (By default, JavaScript caching is enabled)
    
*   **When to Enable**: Only if you encounter a specific issue that requires JavaScript caching to be disabled.
    
*   **Effects**: May slow down page loading. We do not recommend enabling this setting unless necessary.
    

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/advanced-onlymonster-settings-for-troubleshooting#disable-hardware-acceleration)

Disable Hardware Acceleration


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Hardware acceleration shifts certain tasks from your PC’s CPU to the GPU, improving performance in many cases. However, in some situations, it may cause graphical issues or high system load.

*   **Default State:** **Disabled**
    
*   **When to Enable**: If you experience lags, high CPU usage, or graphical glitches while using OnlyFans.
    
*   **Effects**: Forces software rendering, which may reduce the load on weaker PCs and fix graphical issues.
    

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/advanced-onlymonster-settings-for-troubleshooting#how-to-adjust-these-settings)

How to Adjust These Settings


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/advanced-onlymonster-settings-for-troubleshooting#windows)

Windows

Browser settings on Windows can be accessed by right-clicking on the Monster logo:

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252F7csM9rLFHVfB0w7HGq53%252FDisable.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df1ceed4b-55da-434d-9721-e09ce7c13f19&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a4e801e9&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/advanced-onlymonster-settings-for-troubleshooting#macos)

MacOS

On MacOS, you can access settings via menu bar at the top:

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FPTskc2Xuut5qQGmjgiNt%252F%25D0%25A1%25D0%25BD%25D0%25B8%25D0%25BC%25D0%25BE%25D0%25BA%2520%25D1%258D%25D0%25BA%25D1%2580%25D0%25B0%25D0%25BD%25D0%25B0%25202025-04-06%2520%25D0%25B2%252011.33.31.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dadd71d9a-282e-4564-b127-e17b63dc14c8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ca5b8c10&sv=2)

# “Proxy Missing” Error | Onlymonster Docs

The **Proxy Missing** error occurs when there is no active proxy on the creator’s account or if the proxy has been deactivated.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FjUMgNBbVwCIM0XPpjL1Q%252FScreenshot%25202025-03-27%2520at%252012.49.09.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6f35b111-df9a-4686-8575-fcd63a88997a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5b115903&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/proxy-missing-error#understanding-the-issue)

Understanding the Issue

**This error can happen due to the following reasons:**

*   The creator’s account plan has expired for more than 72 hours, leading to proxy deactivation.
    
*   The process of adding the creator was interrupted and not completed.
    

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/proxy-missing-error#solution)

Solution

**To resolve the “Proxy Missing” error, follow these steps:**

1.  Go to the **Creators** tab.
    
2.  Click on **Open Settings** for the creator with the issue.
    

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FPdGTOKEEKfLxmICOPB7x%252FScreenshot%25202025-03-27%2520at%252012.50.59.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D85d8911c-35dd-4bbf-ba15-110bf2f9793c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=918cc662&sv=2)

1.  Navigate to **Proxy Settings** and select a proxy to activate.
    

*   We recommend choosing a Primary Proxy from the nearest location: **Germany**, **Singapore**, or the **USA**.
    
*   An icon labeled **Selected** will appear next to the chosen proxy. Ensure you’ve selected the closest proxy to your location.
    

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FDtFYRFURic7eUGL5RC0j%252FScreenshot%25202025-03-27%2520at%252012.53.05.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9a42017d-ed92-43ee-bfb2-15e0868f9d54&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=96111e86&sv=2)

For more details on proxy settings, review the article [Proxy Management](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/onlymonster-browser/proxy-management)

If you need further assistance, please contact our support team.

[Next"Allow 3 seconds" Error](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/allow-3-seconds-error)

# "Allow 3 seconds" Error | Onlymonster Docs

The **"Allow 3 seconds" error** is a system message from OnlyFans that appears when attempting to send certain requests too frequently (e.g. publishing posts and sending direct/priority messages more often than OnlyFans allows).

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FSSqoam3LfrvVY5m6qJmm%252Fallow%25203%2520sec.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7bd1670e-3964-4dbf-9c84-9384b6335955&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=515a70a5&sv=2)

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/allow-3-seconds-error#understanding-the-issue)

Understanding the Issue


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This error occurs due to the following reasons:

*   Publishing posts and sending direct/priority messages too frequently.
    
*   There is an incorrect Time Delay in Priority Mass Messages
    

OnlyFans limits the frequency of certain actions to ensure they are performed by a single creator in a natural manner. The platform restricts some requests to once every 3 seconds, assuming that one person cannot perform multiple actions within that timeframe.

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/allow-3-seconds-error#priority-mass-messages-and-incorrect-time-delay)

Priority Mass Messages & Incorrect Time Delay

*   The Priority Mass Messages feature sends individual private messages to each fan with a customizable time interval.
    
*   If the time interval is set too short, OnlyFans may detect it as spam and trigger the "Allow 3 Seconds" error.
    

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/allow-3-seconds-error#share-for-share-sfs-limitations)

Share-for-Share (SFS) Limitations

*   The OnlyFans system does not differentiate between scheduled and regular publishing.
    
*   If multiple SFS posts are scheduled too close together, the system may flag them, resulting in errors.
    

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/allow-3-seconds-error#solutions)

Solutions


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Identify the Cause of the Error
    

*   If the error occurs due to multiple actions performed at the same time, prioritize the most important action and pause the others temporarily.
    

1.  Adjust the Time Delay in Priority Mass Messages
    

*   If sending to 450 fans or fewer, set the time delay to 3 seconds per message.
    
*   If sending to more than 450 fans, increase the delay to at least 4-5 seconds to prevent system detection as spam.
    

By following these adjustments, you can avoid disruptions, ensure messages are sent successfully, and comply with OnlyFans' limits.

[Previous“Proxy Missing” Error](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/proxy-missing-error)
[Next“Too many requests. Try again later” Error](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/too-many-requests.-try-again-later-error)

# “Just a Moment...” Loading Screen | Onlymonster Docs

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FqmPzkPjvqrfBoers45jm%252F15%2520src%2520.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Defd1112c-4788-484b-9fa4-0f031607c27e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ff2709ce&sv=2)

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/just-a-moment...-loading-screen#understanding-the-issue)

Understanding the Issue


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The loading screen may appear due to various reasons.

1.  **Server connection**
    

OnlyFans is attempting to establish a connection with the server. This is part of the platform’s security and verification process.

1.  **Unstable Network**
    

A slow or interrupted internet connection can cause prolonged loading times.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/just-a-moment...-loading-screen#solution)

Solution


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  **Wait**
    

In most cases, the page will load automatically within 15–30 seconds.

1.  **Refresh the Page**
    

Press Ctrl + R (Windows) or Cmd + R (Mac) to reload the page.

1.  **Change Network**
    

Switch from Wi-Fi to mobile data (or vice versa) to rule out local connectivity issues.

1.  **Switch Proxies**
    

Try changing your proxy. See [instructions here](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/onlymonster-browser/proxy-management)
.

1.  **Enable VPN**
    

Turn on your VPN and refresh the page.

If you still encounter the error after trying these steps, please contact our support team.

# “Wrong Creator” Error When Attempting to Log Into a Profile | Onlymonster Docs

**Users encounter a “Wrong Creator” error message when trying to log into a model's profile.**

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/wrong-creator-error-when-attempting-to-log-into-a-profile#symptoms)

Symptoms

An error message stating “Wrong Creator” appears during the login process.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fstorage.crisp.chat%2Fusers%2Fhelpdesk%2Fwebsite%2Fe976c4b45fb54800%2Fimage_8060cd.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5323d163&sv=2)

"Wrong Creator" error message

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/wrong-creator-error-when-attempting-to-log-into-a-profile#solutions)

Solutions

1.  **Check Selected Icon**
    

Ensure the correct profile picture is selected on the left side of the interface.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fstorage.crisp.chat%2Fusers%2Fhelpdesk%2Fwebsite%2Fe976c4b45fb54800%2Fksnip20240527-154741_14yu0is.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1046cca8&sv=2)

Verify profile photos

1.  **Free and Paid Page Accounts**
    

If accessing a model with both Free and Paid pages, verify that they are registered on OnlyFans as two separate accounts with distinct login credentials.

1.  **Verify Login Credentials**
    

Double-check the username and password you are using. They may belong to a different account.

1.  **Contact Support**
    

If steps 1 to 3 do not resolve the issue, reach out to our support team for further assistance.

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/wrong-creator-error-when-attempting-to-log-into-a-profile#additional-tips)

Additional Tips

*   Always keep your login information secure and up-to-date.
    
*   Regularly update your browser or app to ensure compatibility.
    

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/wrong-creator-error-when-attempting-to-log-into-a-profile#contact-for-further-assistance)

Contact for Further Assistance

For further help or if you experience other issues, please contact our support team.

# “DiscardVirtualMemory” Error | Onlymonster Docs

**Users encounter a “DiscardVirtualMemory” error message, likely due to operating system incompatibility.**

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/discardvirtualmemory-error#understanding-the-issue)

Understanding the Issue

The **“DiscardVirtualMemory”** error is often related to software attempting to use a function or feature not supported by older operating systems, such as Windows 7 or 8.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fstorage.crisp.chat%2Fusers%2Fhelpdesk%2Fwebsite%2Fe976c4b45fb54800%2F2024-05-27-13-34-24_bcxt4x.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=cb5c49f6&sv=2)

Discard Virtual Memory - Update your OS

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/discardvirtualmemory-error#solutions)

Solutions

1.  **Check Operating System Compatibility**
    

*   Verify your operating system version. The error usually occurs on Windows 7 or Windows 8.
    
*   Upgrade Operating System: Our browser supports only Windows 10+ and MacOS. Please update your system to a compatible version.
    

1.  **Contact Support**
    

If you need assistance with upgrading your operating system or if you have other related queries, please reach out to the support team for further assistance.

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/discardvirtualmemory-error#additional-tips)

Additional Tips

Before upgrading your system, ensure your hardware meets the minimum requirements for Windows 10 or the latest MacOS version. Always back up important data before performing an operating system upgrade.

# “Captcha wrong” error | Onlymonster Docs

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/captcha-wrong-error#understanding-the-issue)

Understanding the Issue


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The "Captcha wrong" error appears when attempting to pass the captcha during the login process for the Creator account. This issue may occur even if the captcha is successfully completed.

Don't make many attempts when this error happens, OnlyFans has limits on the number of attempts.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252Fi4hv80rb25D83wqTIXRQ%252FCW.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D69575192-81c2-4b66-8b56-9893043ce125&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=847372b1&sv=2)

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/captcha-wrong-error#solutions)

Solutions


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The issue can be resolved by temporarily changing the proxy to Singapore. After completing the CAPTCHA, it is essential (!) to **switch the proxy back**.

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/captcha-wrong-error#step-by-step-instructions)

Step-by-step instructions

1.  Switch proxy to Singapore
    

Go to [**Creators**](https://onlymonster.ai/panel/creators/)
 → **Open Settings** → **Proxy** settings and change the proxy to **Singapore**.

1.  Retry completing captcha
    

After switching the proxy, **attempt to pass the captcha** again.

1.  Contact support
    

If the error persists after trying these steps, contact our support team.

1.  Switch proxy back after completing the captcha
    

Set the proxy used before the switch. We recommend to set up proxy with the closest country to chatter. You can read more about proxy management in our [article](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/onlymonster-browser/proxy-management)
.

[Previous“DiscardVirtualMemory” Error](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/discardvirtualmemory-error)
[Next“Something Went Wrong” Error](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/something-went-wrong-error)

Last updated 7 months ago

# OnlyMonster Browser Troubleshooting Guide | Onlymonster Docs

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/onlymonster-browser-troubleshooting-guide#onlymonster-browser-wont-run)

OnlyMonster Browser won't run


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/onlymonster-browser-troubleshooting-guide#id-1.-reboot-your-computer)

1\. Reboot Your Computer

Rebooting your computer periodically helps applications run faster and more smoothly. If the browser doesn’t launch, **reboot your PC** and try again.

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/onlymonster-browser-troubleshooting-guide#id-2.-check-your-operating-system)

2\. Check Your Operating System

OnlyMonster Browser is optimized for **Windows 10** and **macOS 11.0** or later. If you're using an older version, please update your operating system to the required version.

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/onlymonster-browser-troubleshooting-guide#id-3.-check-for-antivirus-or-firewall-interference)

3\. Check for Antivirus or Firewall Interference

Antivirus or firewall software may block the browser for the following reasons:

**— Blocking executable files**: Some antivirus programs mistakenly flag the browser as unsafe and block it.

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/onlymonster-browser-troubleshooting-guide#to-resolve-this)

To resolve this:

**— Disable your antivirus and firewalls**: Temporarily turn off your antivirus and firewall to check if they’re causing the issue. For Windows users, ensure that **Windows Defender Antivirus** and **Windows Firewall** are also disabled. Follow these steps:

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/onlymonster-browser-troubleshooting-guide#how-to-disable-windows-defender-antivirus)

How to Disable Windows Defender Antivirus:

*   Open the **Start Menu** and search for **Windows Security**.
    
*   Click on **Virus & Threat Protection**.
    
*   Under **Virus & Threat Protection Settings**, click **Manage Settings**.
    
*   Toggle off **Real-time protection** to temporarily disable Windows Defender.
    

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/onlymonster-browser-troubleshooting-guide#how-to-disable-windows-firewall)

How to Disable Windows Firewall:

*   Open the **Start Menu** and search for **Windows Defender Firewall**.
    
*   Click on **Turn Windows Defender Firewall on or off** in the left panel.
    
*   Select **Turn off Windows Defender Firewall** for both **Private** and **Public** network settings.
    

After disabling the antivirus and firewall, try launching OnlyMonster Browser again.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/onlymonster-browser-troubleshooting-guide#gray-screen-after-launching-browser)

Gray Screen After Launching Browser


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If the browser opens but displays a gray screen and doesn’t load further, try the following:

*   Ensure your antivirus and firewall are **disabled** (as described above).
    
*   Check your internet connection: make sure your connection is stable and meets the minimum speed requirement of **50 Mbps**.
    
*   **Verify your internet service provider is not blocking the browser**: try connecting through a different network or using a VPN.
    

* * *

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/onlymonster-browser-troubleshooting-guide#other-common-errors)

Other Common Errors


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/onlymonster-browser-troubleshooting-guide#type-1-sidebar-loaded-but-onlyfans-profiles-not-displaying)

Type 1: Sidebar Loaded, but OnlyFans Profiles Not Displaying

If the sidebar loads but OnlyFans profiles do not display and the OnlyMonster loader keeps freezing:

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fstorage.crisp.chat%2Fusers%2Fhelpdesk%2Fwebsite%2Fe976c4b45fb54800%2Ftrblst_pzpjpl.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2b9cde72&sv=2)

*   **Disable OnlyFans Proxy Bypass**: Go to **OnlyMonsterAI > Settings > Disable OnlyFans Proxy Bypass**. (On Windows OS, right-click the monster icon to find the settings.)
    

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fstorage.crisp.chat%2Fusers%2Fhelpdesk%2Fwebsite%2Fe976c4b45fb54800%2Fscreenshot-2024-09-13-at-14432_1d4hffq.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d5582568&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/onlymonster-browser-troubleshooting-guide#type-2-sidebar-loaded-but-profile-pages-stuck-on-gray-screen)

Type 2: Sidebar Loaded, but Profile Pages Stuck on Gray Screen

*   For macOS: Delete the application and download it again.
    
*   For Windows: Close the application, open Task Manager, and end all processes associated with OnlyMonster Browser. Then, restart the application.
    

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fstorage.crisp.chat%2Fusers%2Fhelpdesk%2Fwebsite%2Fe976c4b45fb54800%2Fomscr7-1_10tprfs.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1b6d8d20&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/onlymonster-browser-troubleshooting-guide#type-3-update-check-failed-error-on-windows)

Type 3: “Update Check Failed” Error on Windows

If you encounter this error, click the Run anyway link to proceed.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fstorage.crisp.chat%2Fusers%2Fhelpdesk%2Fwebsite%2Fe976c4b45fb54800%2Fupdate-check-failed_1sh2s65.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=283731f7&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/onlymonster-browser-troubleshooting-guide#type-4-error-loading-application-data)

Type 4: “Error Loading Application Data”

If this error occurs, close the application, wait 5-10 minutes, and then reopen it. This is a temporary issue that may occur after system updates.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fstorage.crisp.chat%2Fusers%2Fhelpdesk%2Fwebsite%2Fe976c4b45fb54800%2Fqq_1nopr9o.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b6ef84db&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/onlymonster-browser-troubleshooting-guide#type-5-proxy-issues)

Type 5: Proxy Issues

If there is an error related to proxies, you need to change the proxy settings:

1.  Navigate to the Creators tab.
    
2.  Open Settings.
    
3.  In the Proxy Settings panel, click Switch IP or change the proxy to another country.
    
4.  Restart the browser.
    

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fstorage.crisp.chat%2Fusers%2Fhelpdesk%2Fwebsite%2Fe976c4b45fb54800%2Fproxy_1bzvagd.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e19f2a44&sv=2)

For more information on Proxy settings, please refer to the Proxy Management article.

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/onlymonster-browser-troubleshooting-guide#still-having-issues)

Still Having Issues?

If the problem persists, please contact our technical support team for further assistance.

[NextAdvanced OnlyMonster Settings for troubleshooting](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/advanced-onlymonster-settings-for-troubleshooting)

# “Something Went Wrong” Error | Onlymonster Docs

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FZu5u3zoZdEuTvufm4Hhz%252FScreenshot%25202025-03-24%2520at%252012.56.47.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4477edd3-7772-4942-8b47-fd1e3b707ed8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=bd38d7ba&sv=2)

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/something-went-wrong-error#understanding-the-issue)

Understanding the Issue


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

OnlyFans can **temporarily or permanently restrict access to certain actions.**

This may happen for several reasons, including **short-term issues or extended account limitations.**

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/something-went-wrong-error#solution)

Solution


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1\. Check if the issue also appears when using OnlyFans directly (outside the CRM).

2\. If the error occurs on the OnlyFans platform as well, please contact OnlyFans Support to resolve the issue.

If you have any further questions, feel free to reach out to our support team—we’re here to help.

[Previous“Captcha wrong” error](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/captcha-wrong-error)
[Next“Just a Moment...” Loading Screen](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/just-a-moment...-loading-screen)

# Forgot Password | Onlymonster Docs

**Resetting your password**

1.  Click on your **profile icon** in the upper right corner.
    
2.  Choose **Sign Out** to open the login screen.
    

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252F5twuFNHStjiPWJK3MDt1%252FScreenshot%25202025-03-24%2520at%252015.00.27.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Deb4959e1-eca9-4df9-a82f-4efa4b7840c9&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=94cacfbb&sv=2)

1.  On the login screen, select **Forgot Password?**
    

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FPricfeBDo4dNK0aR121K%252FScreenshot%25202025-03-24%2520at%252015.07.21.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcaa1aa23-3e32-4a5f-9844-024bcfca8758&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a0ebe844&sv=2)

1.  This will open a browser window. Enter your email and select **Forgot Password?**
    
2.  Choose **Reset your password**.
    

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FcU3em14JseRt0vUfrq4n%252FScreenshot%25202025-03-24%2520at%252015.10.45.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0b924f23-144b-421c-b13a-1dd91b13a164&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f3bc6fbc&sv=2)

1.  OnlyMonster will send you a code to change the password, which you need to enter.
    
2.  Create and confirm your new password.
    

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FSOeGior1PBIOK8amXK7m%252FScreenshot%25202025-03-24%2520at%252015.11.28.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dca50c38b-1907-4130-bf36-b61d4bfa2f0e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fe92c190&sv=2)

Your password is now changed, and you’ll need to log in with the new password.

If you have an Auto-Save Password feature enabled, you can change your password directly in the Manage Account menu. For more details on updating your password or other account information, check out our article Manage Account Information.

[PreviousAdvanced OnlyMonster Settings for troubleshooting](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/advanced-onlymonster-settings-for-troubleshooting)
[Next“Proxy Missing” Error](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/proxy-missing-error)

# Payment Guide | Onlymonster Docs

**Payment can be made with** [**cryptocurrency**](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/billing-and-pricing/payment-guide#cryptocurrency-payment)
 **or** [**bank card**](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/billing-and-pricing/payment-guide#credit-card-payment)
**.**

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/billing-and-pricing/payment-guide#summary)

Summary


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Making payments and extending subscriptions, as well as purchasing AI credits on OnlyMonster can be done according to the following scheme:

1.  **Add funds to your agency balance** using a credit card or cryptocurrency.
    
2.  **Renew creator plans** by selecting the appropriate plan and making payment or **Purchase additional AI credits** when needed.
    

A **red notification** appearing in the **Billing tab** indicates that a **renewal is due**. The counter shows the number of accounts whose plan is about to **expire**. The notification appears 3 days before the plan expires.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FU9iKm4vVCwWPKUFfyiPq%252Fimage%2520%289%29%2520%281%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6a715249-fe03-4c8c-9ed9-01f3b7abbdb9&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d1b2b758&sv=2)

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/billing-and-pricing/payment-guide#adding-funds-to-your-agency-balance)

Adding Funds to Your Agency Balance


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Before extending plans or purchasing additional AI credits, funds need to be credited to your agency balance.

Navigate to the [Billing tab](https://onlymonster.ai/panel/billing/)
 - **Add Funds To Your Balance**.

Specify the exact amount that will be added to your **Agency Balance**.

Choose the preferred Payment method: **Credit Card** or **Cryptocurrency**.

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/billing-and-pricing/payment-guide#credit-card-payment)

Credit Card Payment

1.  Enter the **required card details** (card number, expiration date, CVV, and other details required by the payment system).
    
2.  After payment is processed, you’ll receive an **invoice by email**.
    

In case of a pending or unsuccessful transaction you’ll receive an email from the payment system (contact our support for further assistance)

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/billing-and-pricing/payment-guide#cryptocurrency-payment)

Cryptocurrency Payment

1.  Select your preferred **cryptocurrency** and **network**.
    
2.  Copy the provided **payment address** or scan the **QR code**.
    
3.  Open your **cryptocurrency wallet** and **complete the transaction**.
    

Be sure to consider any network's commissions and fees.

It may take up to 10 minutes for funds to be credited to your account.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/billing-and-pricing/payment-guide#extending-creators-plans)

Extending Creators’ Plans


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Once your agency account has sufficient funds, you can extend the subscription plans for your creators.

Plan duration: Each subscription lasts 30 days.

1.  In the **Billing tab**, go to the **Subscriptions section**.
    
2.  **Locate the creator** whose plan you want to renew.
    
3.  Choose a renewal duration: 1-month, 3-month, or 6-month
    

Available options depend on the creator's earnings status. If the creator has no earnings history within the last 30 days, only a 1-month plan is available.

1.  **A plan marked as green indicates you've selected that creator for renewal.** If it’s not marked greed, the plan will not be renewed.
    
2.  Click **Make Payment.**
    

For now, we do not support recurring payments, all payments should be made manually.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/billing-and-pricing/payment-guide#purchasing-additional-ai-credits)

Purchasing Additional AI Credits


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In case additional **AI credits** are needed, you can easily purchase more through the **Billing tab**:

1.  Click **Purchase More AI Credits**.
    
2.  Select the **number of credits** you want to purchase.
    
3.  Confirm your purchase and proceed with payment.
    

Once processed, your AI credits will be automatically replenished.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/billing-and-pricing/payment-guide#troubleshooting-payment-issues)

Troubleshooting Payment Issues


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you encounter any issues with payments (for example, if funds aren’t appearing in your account), here's what to do:

*   **For Credit Card Payments:** Check your email for a **receipt from the payment system**, and contact our support.
    
*   **For Cryptocurrency Payments:** If your funds haven’t appeared, share the **Transaction ID (TxID)** with our support for faster assistance.
    

[PreviousPlans and Pricing](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/billing-and-pricing/plans-and-pricing)
[NextOnlyMonster Browser Troubleshooting Guide](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/troubleshooting/onlymonster-browser-troubleshooting-guide)

Last updated 8 months ago

Was this helpful?

# OnlyMonster Referral System | Onlymonster Docs

The OnlyMonster Referral System rewards you for inviting new agencies to the platform. When an agency registers using your referral link, you earn a commission, and they get an extended trial period.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/billing-and-pricing/onlymonster-referral-system#how-it-works)

How It Works


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Every agency member has access to the referral system, no matter their role.
    
*   Each member has a **unique referral code and link**, assigned personally to them.
    
*   When a new agency registers using your link, they receive an extended free trial for all profiles added within 10 days of registration.
    

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FKQqfcxqex3YxQV7siTdc%252FScreenshot%25202025-06-25%2520at%252013.25.15.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0db28d87-2458-4531-9d1a-ed93549e1c94&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=88d409e&sv=2)

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/billing-and-pricing/onlymonster-referral-system#referral-tiers)

Referral Tiers


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The referral system includes two levels:

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/billing-and-pricing/onlymonster-referral-system#level-1-direct-referrals)

Level 1: Direct Referrals:

*   These are agencies that register using your referral link or code.
    
*   You receive **10% of all their balance top-ups** for the next **365 days**.
    

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/billing-and-pricing/onlymonster-referral-system#level-2-indirect-referrals)

Level 2: Indirect Referrals:

*   These are agencies invited by your **Level 1 referrals**.
    
*   You receive **2% of their balance top-ups,** also for **365 days**.
    

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/billing-and-pricing/onlymonster-referral-system#fund-withdrawal)

Fund Withdrawal


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Referral rewards can be used in two ways:

1.  **Transfer to Agency Balance** \- Instantly move earned funds to your agency account balance and use them to pay for OnlyMonster services.
    
2.  **Cryptocurrency Withdrawal** \- Withdraw your referral earnings directly to your crypto wallet.
    

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/billing-and-pricing/onlymonster-referral-system#inviting-referrals)

Inviting Referrals


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To invite an agency, you can either:

*   **Copy your referral link** and share it directly
    
*   Or send your **referral code** for manual entry
    

During the registration process, the invited agency must paste your referral code into the designated field.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FH4E5ovUowQwDUWd1S8pR%252FScreenshot%25202025-06-25%2520at%252013.32.22.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De8342d41-375a-4563-8040-d8aac676f58a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=48674833&sv=2)

Agencies that register using your referral link or code receive an **extended 14-day trial** for all creators added within 10 days of registration.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/billing-and-pricing/onlymonster-referral-system#overview-dashboard)

Overview Dashboard


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FGymhCwlMYpH65Tk46HoG%252FScreenshot%25202025-06-25%2520at%252013.15.46.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1d1b828d-46c4-4182-a53b-3f12a633d9f8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8b629df9&sv=2)

The Overview tab in the Referral system displays key stats:

1.  **Total Revenue** - Lifetime earnings from all referrals (Level 1 and 2)
    
2.  **Withdrawn Funds** - Total funds already withdrawn (agency balance + crypto)
    
3.  **Lvl 1 Referrals** \- Number of direct (Level 1) referrals
    
4.  **Lvl 2 Referrals** - Number of indirect (Level 2) referrals
    
5.  **Lvl 1 Revenue** - Earnings from Level 1 referrals
    
6.  **Lvl 2 Revenue** - Earnings from Level 2 referrals
    
7.  **Current Balance** - Referral earnings available for withdrawal
    
8.  **Withdraw Button** \- Click to access withdrawal options
    

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/billing-and-pricing/onlymonster-referral-system#balance-withdrawal)

Balance Withdrawal


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To withdraw your referral earnings, click the **Withdraw** button in the Overview tab. A popup window will appear with two options:

*   **Transfer to Agency Balance**
    
*   **Withdraw to Crypto Wallet**
    

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FGjxs8rs9K7bf7x6zadUS%252FScreenshot%25202025-06-25%2520at%252013.20.17.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dea35f72e-fe8e-42ba-b279-b29d5de83521&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3a6286dc&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/billing-and-pricing/onlymonster-referral-system#withdrawal-to-agency-balance)

Withdrawal to Agency Balance

Withdrawal to your agency account is processed without any fees. The minimum withdrawal amount is $100.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252Fr5ERXTPB4nUc3iETDEcN%252FScreenshot%25202025-06-25%2520at%252013.21.53.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8b324292-7f25-42d6-800f-6fac34e15ac2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=cbf71623&sv=2)

To withdraw funds:

1.  Enter the amount in the input field (or click "Max" to withdraw your full balance)
    
2.  Click **Submit**
    

Your request will be marked as **Pending** and sent for review. After approval, the funds will be credited to your **Agency Balance.**

Once processed, the transaction will appear in your Billing History and be reflected in your agency balance.

If your request is stuck in “Pending” or gets canceled, contact our support team for clarification.

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/billing-and-pricing/onlymonster-referral-system#withdrawal-to-crypto-wallet)

Withdrawal to Crypto Wallet

To withdraw funds to your crypto wallet, click the **Withdraw** button and select crypto wallet withdrawal. We do not charge any fees for this operation, however network fees may apply.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FC03N5N1bIGvaVULlE2p6%252FScreenshot%25202025-06-25%2520at%252013.02.24.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D906fa06f-3b1d-4825-b7a1-659f5adfa01c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=97cf01ef&sv=2)

To complete the withdrawal:

1.  Enter the exact withdrawal amount (minimum $100)
    
2.  Choose a stablecoin: USDT or USDC
    
3.  Choose the appropriate network from the dropdown menu
    
4.  Enter your wallet address
    
5.  Add comments if necessary
    
6.  Click **Submit**
    

Funds are usually transferred within 2-3 business days.

For changes, corrections, or delayed transactions, please contact our support team.

[PreviousBoosting Fan Engagement with AI-Powered Priority Mass Messages](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/ai-magic-assistant/boosting-fan-engagement-with-ai-powered-priority-mass-messages)
[NextPlans and Pricing](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/billing-and-pricing/plans-and-pricing)
