# AI Suggestions: A Guide to AI Modes | Onlymonster Docs

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/ai-magic-assistant/ai-suggestions-a-guide-to-ai-modes#how-ai-suggestions-works)

How AI Suggestions Works

AI Suggestions analyzes your **chat history** (up to the last 15 messages) and generates tailored responses that:

*   **Continue the natural flow** of your conversation
    
*   **Mirror your messaging style** precisely, including message length, emoji use, and punctuation patterns
    
*   **Match the current tone and intimacy level** based on the chat history
    
*   Provide **one ready-to-send message** with no extra labels or meta-text
    

Simply select the mode that fits your goal, and the AI will generate an appropriate response based on your conversation context.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252F32hSMsE5JOLHL6qdy309%252Ftg_image_929255678.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D083c20ec-fc3a-477c-a736-3631a29c83f1&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e2dcd26d&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/ai-magic-assistant/ai-suggestions-a-guide-to-ai-modes#quick-access-ai-modes)

Quick Access AI Modes

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/ai-magic-assistant/ai-suggestions-a-guide-to-ai-modes#quick-reply)

Quick Reply

**What it does:** Continues the exact flow of your chat with short, natural responses that match your style, punctuation, and emoji use.

**Best for:** Maintaining conversation momentum with quick, authentic replies that feel natural.

**Key features:**

*   Mirrors your style precisely
    
*   Keeps the conversation moving
    
*   No greetings, topic shifts, or meta-text
    
*   Based entirely on your chat history patterns
    

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/ai-magic-assistant/ai-suggestions-a-guide-to-ai-modes#engage-questions)

Engage (Questions)

**What it does:** Generates one playful, context-sensitive question or mini-challenge anchored to the fan's last message to re-hook their attention

**Best for:** Re-engaging fans and sparking interaction when the conversation slows down.

**Key features:**

*   Anchored to the fan’s last message
    
*   Fun, relevant, and specific — never generic
    
*   No interview-style or hypothetical questions
    
*   Designed to spark immediate interaction
    

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/ai-magic-assistant/ai-suggestions-a-guide-to-ai-modes#innocent)

Innocent

**What it does:** Provides a bashful, naive, or modest response that contrasts with the current chat tone.

**Best for:** Adding emotional variety, creating contrast, or cooling down intensity

**Key features:**

*   Shows expressive innocence with variety
    
*   Keeps the thread moving forward
    
*   Uses "double-layer innocence" in NSFW contexts
    
*   Avoids infantilization or repetitive phrases
    

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/ai-magic-assistant/ai-suggestions-a-guide-to-ai-modes#playful)

Playful

**What it does:** Creates cheeky, bold, and unpredictable hooks that keep fans engaged without going fully NSFW.

**Best for:** Teasing and keeping the chat fun, light, and unpredictable.

**Key features:**

*   Interactive, specific, and magnetic
    
*   Strong, engaging endings
    
*   No paraphrasing or bland small talk
    

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/ai-magic-assistant/ai-suggestions-a-guide-to-ai-modes#spicy)

Spicy

**What it does:** Smoothly escalates or intensifies NSFW tension based on the fan's vibe and current chat flow.

**Best for:** Naturally building intimacy when the conversation is heating up

**Key features:**

*   Matches the current intensity level
    
*   "Show, don't ask" approach
    
*   Escalates naturally without abrupt jumps
    
*   Reads subtle cues and bridges naturally into sexting
    
*   Avoids clichés or sudden escalation
    

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/ai-magic-assistant/ai-suggestions-a-guide-to-ai-modes#upsell-sales-unlock)

Upsell (Sales/Unlock)

**What it does:** Generates non-specific teases to trigger purchases — without naming content formats.

**Best for:** Monetizing the conversation when you're ready to sell content

**Key features:**

*   Uses sensory and emotional triggers
    
*   Creates urgency and exclusivity
    
*   Doesn’t mention formats (photo, video, call, etc.)
    
*   Works with any type of content you offer
    

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/ai-magic-assistant/ai-suggestions-a-guide-to-ai-modes#legacy-modes)

Legacy Modes

The following modes are still available for **backward compatibility** but will be merged or removed soon:

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/ai-magic-assistant/ai-suggestions-a-guide-to-ai-modes#question)

Question

Overlaps with Engage; often produces generic questions. **Will be merged into Engage (Questions).**

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/ai-magic-assistant/ai-suggestions-a-guide-to-ai-modes#ppv)

PPV

Overlaps with Upsell; seen as mass promotion. **Will be merged into Upsell (Sales/Unlock).**

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/ai-magic-assistant/ai-suggestions-a-guide-to-ai-modes#bullet)

Bullet

Short messages duplicating Quick Reply/Playful functionality. **Will be removed soon.**

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/ai-magic-assistant/ai-suggestions-a-guide-to-ai-modes#bump)

Bump

Meme-like "wake-up" nudges similar to Quick Reply. **Will be removed soon.**

These modes overlap with **the updated ones** and can create confusion. The refreshed modes provide clearer options and better results.

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/ai-magic-assistant/ai-suggestions-a-guide-to-ai-modes#message-requirements)

Message Requirements

To get the best results from AI Suggestions, ensure there are at least 5 incoming messages **in your chat history.** This allows the AI to:

*   Understand the conversation context
    
*   Mirror your style accurately
    
*   Match the current tone and flow
    
*   Generate relevant, natural responses
    

**Note:** The AI prioritizes the **latest fan message and immediate thread** to keep responses contextual and timely.

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/ai-magic-assistant/ai-suggestions-a-guide-to-ai-modes#tips-for-best-results)

Tips for Best Results

**Choose the right mode for your goal:**

*   Need a natural continuation? → **Quick Reply**
    
*   Want to re-engage attention? → **Engage (Questions)**
    
*   Need emotional variety or cooldown? → **Innocent**
    
*   Want to tease without going NSFW? → **Playful**
    
*   Ready to escalate intimacy? → **Spicy**
    
*   Time to monetize? → **Upsell (Sales/Unlock)**
    

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FWILHkAvToaezHnEPaWeF%252F4444.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1eccbdfd-ea38-4e9f-b729-c794bdef17f2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b56963ab&sv=2)

**Provide enough context:** The AI works best with **10-15 recent messages** in chat history. More context = better, more personalized suggestions.

**Switch modes if needed:** If a mode feels repetitive, try a different one or add more messages to the thread before generating again.

**Use as-is:** The output is ready to send immediately with no labels or meta-text — just generate and send.

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/ai-magic-assistant/ai-suggestions-a-guide-to-ai-modes#understanding-ai-behavior)

Understanding AI Behavior

**Seamless flow:** Updated modes focus on continuing the current thread without topic resets or generic openings.

**Style matching:** The AI mirrors your recent messaging patterns, including length, emoji use, and punctuation.

**Natural progression:** Tone and intimacy follow the conversation's current level — the AI avoids sudden shifts or intensity changes.

**One message output:** Each mode produces a single, ready-to-send message with strict length constraints optimized for engagement.

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/ai-magic-assistant/ai-suggestions-a-guide-to-ai-modes#customizing-ai-modes)

Customizing AI Modes

**Personalization Options:** All AI Modes can be customized to suit your unique needs. Go to the [AI Assistant](https://onlymonster.ai/panel/ai-assistant)
 section in the OnlyMonster to tailor these settings to your preference.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252F0HF00c86vjmnBin44Bsl%252F%25D0%25B0%25D0%25B0%25D0%25B0.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc4d72935-cdde-4ae2-99fd-ced06b9b69b4&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8d3734&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/ai-magic-assistant/ai-suggestions-a-guide-to-ai-modes#troubleshooting)

Troubleshooting

If something feels off:

1.  **Check your chat history:** Make sure you have at least 10-15 messages for proper context.
    
2.  **Check the mode:** Make sure it matches your goal.
    
3.  **Review conversation flow:** The AI mirrors your recent style. Check your last few messages to see the pattern it's following.
    
4.  Try **a different mode:** Sometimes another mode fits the situation better.
    

**Need help?** When reporting issues to support, include screenshots of your last 10-15 messages and AI mode used so we can understand the context and assist you better. The AI's decisions are directly tied to this conversation history.

# Auto Messages | Onlymonster Docs

Auto Messages is a cloud-based OnlyMonster feature that allows you to automatically send delayed **Welcome Messages** for new subscribers and real-time **Messages for Fans Who Come Online**. A system of advanced filters allows you to fine-tune delivery and improve fan engagement.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/auto-messages#general-information-and-overview)

General Information and Overview


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

On the main **Auto Messages** page, you can select a **Creator** and view all **Auto Messages** campaigns launched for that Creator.

To create a new **Campaign**, first select the **Creator** and click the **New Campaign** button.

The feature offers 2 types of auto messages:

1.  **Delayed messages** for new subscribers:
    

You can create one Welcome Message per Creator to be sent after a new subscription.

1.  **Messages for fans who come online**:
    

You can create multiple messages triggered when fans appear online.

For each campaign, you can configure a flexible delay. The message will be sent within a selected time range, which helps maintain a natural and smooth conversation flow.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/auto-messages#overview-section)

Overview Section


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252Fr0WRbDKJrfO6A8Lim3xC%252FScreenshot%25202025-06-26%2520at%252014.25.47.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfce86bdc-3208-41cb-b015-74f15670e455&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8046c352&sv=2)

The following information is displayed in the campaign overview:

*   **Message** - The content of the message
    
*   **Status** - Current state of the campaign:
    
    *   **Active** - the campaign is running and messages are being sent based on the selected filters
        
    *   **Paused** - the campaign is temporarily stopped. Messages are not being sent but can be resumed at any time.
        
    *   **Archived** - The campaign is inactive and permanently disabled. Once a campaign is archived, this action cannot be undone.
        
    

_**Status Change**_ _- You can change the campaign status by clicking on Active or Paused._

*   **Trigger** - Defines the type of auto message:
    
    *   **Welcome Message** - Sent to new subscribers
        
    *   **Online Message** -Sent when fans appear online
        
    
*   **Audience Filter:** Displays selected filters for targeting, including sending conditions and exclusion lists.
    
*   **Sent** - Total number of messages successfully sent.
    
*   **Unsent** - Number of unsent messages.
    
*   _**Price**_
    
*   _**Purchases**_
    
*   _**Earnings**_
    
*   **Created by** - The name of the team member who created the Campaign
    

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/auto-messages#setting-up-delayed-welcome-messages)

Setting Up Delayed Welcome Messages


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can set up one Delayed Welcome Message per Creator. This message will be sent to first-time subscribers.

The OnlyMonster Welcome Message works independently from the native OnlyFans Welcome Message. If both are active, new subscribers will receive both messages.

To create a **Welcome Message**, select Creator from the dropdown and click **New Campaign**, then choose **Welcome Messages**.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FB4OsKqbenVWzIzGz2bzc%252FScreenshot%25202025-06-26%2520at%252014.30.27.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D15d7c267-154e-40e6-bdcd-59f4483dc7e0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6e1c83a2&sv=2)

You are now redirected to the **Campaign Settings** tab, where you need to configure the campaign settings.

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/auto-messages#apply-action)

Apply Action

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FsYbIyBOXcIX7bK0u43rL%252FScreenshot%25202025-06-26%2520at%252014.44.00.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbb9f40c1-c340-4c13-b8f8-3a9f0871d158&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2ea0eb5b&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/auto-messages#delay)

Delay

In the **Apply Action** field, you can select a flexible delay within which the message will be sent once the trigger activates.

Flexible delay values:

*   Minimum - 1-3 minutes;
    
*   Maximum - 30-60 minutes.
    

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/auto-messages#time-range)

Time Range

You can also set the specific time range during which the messages are allowed to be sent.

To configure:

1.  Toggle the **Time Range** option ON
    
2.  Set your preferred **start and end time**
    
3.  Choose the time zone:
    

*   **UTC**
    
*   **Agency Time Zone**
    

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/auto-messages#auto-unsend-option)

Auto-Unsend Option

You can enable the **Auto-Unsend** feature within the Apply Action field.

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/auto-messages#fans-audience)

Fans Audience

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FwcExrmlczSyiotf4qNC9%252FScreenshot%25202025-06-26%2520at%252014.46.19.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D870bd00e-25dc-4622-9904-0821dec20038&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=96b13abf&sv=2)

When creating a **Welcome Message** campaign, you can apply the following filters to target your audience more precisely:

Filters for Welcome Messages:

*   **Spent on an Agency** \- Target fans who have previously spent money on other accounts within the agency. Set both minimum and maximum spending amounts (both fields are required).
    
*   **Purchased from Agency** \- Filter fans based on the recency of their purchases from other agency models. Options available:
    
*   Purchases made **less than X days ago**.
    
*   Purchases made **more than X days ago**.
    
*   **Buying Power** **filter** - Target fans based on their assigned Buying Power score (range: 0 to 5).
    

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/auto-messages#exclude-fans)

Exclude Fans

Welcome messages use a fixed 24-hour "Active chats" period and can not be customized. If a chatter initiates a conversation with a new subscriber within this 24-hour window, the Welcome message will not be sent.

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/auto-messages#text-and-emojis)

Text and emojis

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FEWsj5rVHc2zn52h2FHBG%252FScreenshot%25202025-06-26%2520at%252014.48.18.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9622468e-1f21-46c0-8bc4-4cd1a320c729&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fa5df3b4&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/auto-messages#composing-the-welcome-message)

Composing the Welcome Message

*   Enter the **Welcome Message** text in the input field.
    
*   Click the plus (+) icon to open the emoji panel and insert emojis into your message.
    

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/auto-messages#personalization)

Personalization

To insert the fan's name or custom name:

Click the **Dynamic Name** button.

Choose between the following options:

*   **Custom Name** \- Custom name you've manually assigned to the fan (if available)
    
*   **Fan's Name** \- The name from the fan's profile (if available)
    
*   **Fan's Name → Custom Name** - Uses the fan's name first. If unavailable, uses the custom name.
    
*   **Custom Name → Fan's Name** \- Uses the custom name first. If unavailable, uses the fan's profile name.
    

**First Word from Name**

When choosing Fan's Name, enable the toggle to insert only the first word (e.g. first name only) into the message.

**Fallback Name**

If neither a fan name nor a custom name is available, set a Fallback Name. This name will be used to personalize the message instead.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/auto-messages#media-content-and-pricing)

Media Content and Pricing


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can enhance your auto messages with both free and paid media, as well as paid text messages.

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/auto-messages#free-media)

**Free Media**

To include free media in your message:

1.  Navigate to the Free Media section
    
2.  Click the plus (+) button to add media
    
3.  Select content from your media hub (all media must be uploaded to the media hub first)
    

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/auto-messages#paid-media)

**Paid Media**

To create messages with paid media content:

1.  Enable the Paid Media toggle
    
2.  Enter the price in the Price field
    
3.  Click the plus (+) button in the Paid Media section to add content
    

Use a dot (.) for decimal prices (e.g. 3.99, not 3,99).

This feature only works when using the English keyboard layout.

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/auto-messages#paid-text-messages)

**Paid Text Messages**

You can also assign a price to text-only messages:

1.  Enable the Paid Text toggle
    
2.  Enter the desired price in the Text Price field.
    

**Before launching the campaign:**

*   Carefully review all fields and settings.
    
*   Once the campaign is started, neither the message nor the settings can be edited.
    

When everything is verified, click **Start Campaign** to launch.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/auto-messages#setting-up-delayed-auto-messages-for-fans-appearing-online)

Setting Up Delayed Auto Messages for Fans Appearing Online


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Unlike welcome messages (limited to one active campaign per Creator), you can create multiple auto-messaging campaigns for fans appearing online, each with unique filters and settings to better engage different segments of the creator's active audience.

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252F0mC2SSjzVX2zfvFiWvfU%252FScreenshot%25202025-06-26%2520at%252014.40.02.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd0879546-bbe7-4993-ba14-a8f56e8654fe&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7a900755&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/auto-messages#key-logic)

Key Logic

*   Once a fan receives a message from a specific campaign, they will not receive additional messages from the same campaign when they appear online again.
    
*   To continue messaging fans who come online repeatedly, create separate campaigns with different filters and settings.
    

If a fan qualifies for multiple active campaigns at the same time, the system will send only one message from one campaign per trigger activation.

When multiple campaigns are created, priority will be given to the most recently created campaign.

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/auto-messages#apply-action-1)

Apply Action

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FdBV2IPDb1LXrlUii94lH%252FScreenshot%25202025-06-26%2520at%252014.51.18%2520%281%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dad27908f-cb01-4f2f-be54-75ca719ee7d6&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8b6b0620&sv=2)

In the **Apply Action** field you need to select a flexible delay within which the message will be delivered (after the trigger activates).

Flexible delay values:

*   Minimum - 1-3 minutes;
    
*   Maximum - 30-60 minutes.
    

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/auto-messages#time-range-1)

Time Range

You can define the time window within which the messages are allowed to be sent.

To configure:

1.  Toggle the **Time Range** option ON
    
2.  Set the start and end time
    
3.  Choose the time zone:
    

*   **UTC**
    
*   **Agency Time Zone**
    

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/auto-messages#auto-unsend-option-1)

Auto-Unsend option

You can enable the **Auto-Unsend** feature within the Apply Action field.

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/auto-messages#message-resend-option)

Message Resend Option

You can choose to resend the same message to a fan after a set period.

The resend option is only available when the Auto-Unsend feature is enabled.

To configure:

1.  Toggle the **Resend Message** option ON
    
2.  Set the number of days before the message can be sent again
    

*   **Minimum**: 1 day
    
*   **Maximum**: 30 days
    

The message will be resent at a minimum of 24 hours after the resend trigger, not from the original send time.

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/auto-messages#fans-audience-1)

Fans Audience

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252FNkMWLZG5pltIkRfQZWrv%252FScreenshot%25202025-06-26%2520at%252014.57.22.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfd80a0eb-4651-4d67-8c49-3e059865ab02&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=12cd8f3b&sv=2)

When setting up **Auto Messages** for fans appearing online, you can apply a range of filters to fine-tune your audience targeting:

*   **Spent on a Creator between** \- Target fans based on how much they have spent on the Creator's page. When activating this filter, you need to specify both minimum and maximum spend.
    
*   **Spent on Agency between** \- Target fans based on their total spending across all models connected to the agency. When choosing this filter, you need to specify both minimum and maximum spend.
    
*   **Purchased from Creator** \- Filter fans based on recent purchases from the Creator:
    
    *   Purchases made **less than X days ago**.
        
    *   Purchases made **more than X days ago**.
        
    
*   **Purchased from Agency** \- Filter fans based on recent purchases from any agency model:
    
    *   Purchases made **less than X days ago**.
        
    *   Purchases made **more than X days ago**.
        
    
*   **Buying Powe**r - Filter fans based on their assigned Buying Power score (range: 0 to 5).
    

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/auto-messages#exclude-fans-1)

Exclude Fans

![](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3576754298-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJ3tUjWV0i06zjZEIvwPN%252Fuploads%252Fz9uwo2U0YsV40Za19CBe%252FScreenshot%25202025-06-26%2520at%252015.00.02.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Deba8ed72-72cc-4e78-b075-9d3fb044eabf&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b3aa604f&sv=2)

Two options are available for excluding fan categories from the campaign:

*   **Active Chats** toggle - allows for excluding active chats (messages sent by the model only are taken into account). Minimum value - 15 minutes, maximum - 24 hours.
    
*   **Exclude fan lists** - you can select any number of exclusion lists.
    

Exclude lists are refreshed every 30 minutes

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/auto-messages#text-and-emojis-1)

Text and emojis

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/auto-messages#composing-the-message)

Composing the Message

*   Enter your message in the input field.
    
*   Click the plus (+) icon to open the emoji panel and insert emojis.
    

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/auto-messages#personalization-1)

Personalization

To insert the fan's name or custom name:

Click the **Dynamic Name** button.

Choose between the following options:

*   **Custom Name** \- Custom name you've manually assigned to the fan (if available)
    
*   **Fan's Name** \- The name from the fan's profile (if available)
    
*   **Fan's Name → Custom Name** - Uses the fan's name first. If unavailable, uses the custom name.
    
*   **Custom Name → Fan's Name** \- Uses the custom name first. If unavailable, uses the fan's profile name.
    

**First Word from Name**

When choosing Fan's Name, enable the toggle to insert only the first word (e.g. first name only) into the message.

**Fallback Name**

If neither a fan name nor a custom name is available, set a **Fallback Name**. This name will be used to personalize the message instead.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/auto-messages#media-content-and-pricing-1)

Media Content and Pricing


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can enhance your auto messages with both free and paid media, as well as paid text messages.

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/auto-messages#free-media-1)

**Free Media**

To include free media in your message:

1.  Navigate to the Free Media section
    
2.  Click the plus (+) button to add media
    
3.  Select content from your media hub (all media must be uploaded to the media hub first)
    

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/auto-messages#paid-media-1)

**Paid Media**

To create messages with paid media content:

1.  Enable the Paid Media toggle
    
2.  Enter the price in the Price field
    
3.  Click the plus (+) button in the Paid Media section to add content
    

Use a dot (.) for decimal prices (e.g. 3.99, not 3,99).

This feature only works when using the English keyboard layout.

### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/auto-messages#paid-text-messages-1)

**Paid Text Messages**

You can also assign a price to text-only messages:

1.  Enable the Paid Text toggle
    
2.  Enter the desired price in the Text Price field.
    

**Before launching the campaign:**

*   Review all fields and settings carefully.
    
*   Once launched, neither the message nor campaign settings can be edited.
    

When ready, click Start Campaign to launch.

After launch, the campaign will appear in the Active status within the campaign list.

[PreviousAgency Settings](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/management-system/agency-settings)
[NextPriority Mass Messages V2.0](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/chatter-features/priority-mass-messages-v2.0)

Last updated 23 days ago

Was this helpful?

*   **Assigning profiles to team members**
    
*   **Shift-based access**
    
*   **Message counter**
    
*   **Desktop push notifications**
    
*   **Roles and permissions management**
    

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/changelog/changelog-2025#july-24-version-3.17.0)

July 24 – Version 3.17.0


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/changelog/changelog-2025#features-19)

Features

**OnlyFans Mass Message Unsend:** Users can now unsend OnlyFans mass messages directly via Statistics → Engagement → Messages → Mass Messages. To unsend mass messages, the OF Mass Messages permission is required (the OF Statistics permission is no longer needed for this action).

**OnlyFans Mass Message Sender Name in Statistics:** The sender name for OnlyFans mass messages is now displayed in OnlyFans Mass Message Statistics (Statistics → Engagement → Messages → Mass Messages).

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/changelog/changelog-2025#july-23-version-3.16.1)

July 23 - Version 3.16.1


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/changelog/changelog-2025#bug-fixes-18)

**Bug Fixes**

**URL Links:** Fixed issue with copied chat links displaying incorrectly. URLs now show the correct link when copied.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/changelog/changelog-2025#july-21-version-3.16.0)

July 21 - Version 3.16.0


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/changelog/changelog-2025#improvements-28)

Improvements

**Media Upload Permission**: Uploads are now restricted during OnlyFans media editing. Users without Add (Upload) New Media permission cannot upload photos during this time.

**Collection Management**: Clear & Delete Label is now available to all users, regardless of Chat Hiding & Fan Blocking permission.

**Content Filtering**: The Restricted Words feature now applies to Quick Reply messages.

**Browser Performance**: Fixed issues with search functionality and preserving the tab state after refreshing the page.

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/changelog/changelog-2025#bug-fixes-19)

Bug Fixes

**Media Hub:** Fixed MediaHub modal positioning that previously blocked interaction with the background interface.

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/changelog/changelog-2025#july-15-version-3.15.0)

July 15 - Version 3.15.0


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/changelog/changelog-2025#features-20)

Features

**Chat scrolling:** Implemented workaround to preserve scroll position when reaching the top of an OnlyFans chat.

#### 

[](https://docs.onlymonster.ai/changelog/changelog-2025#improvements-29)

Improvements

**Profile labels and Spend badges:** Improved message URL matching using regex constants for more accurate rendering of profile labels and spend badges.
